prāṇāntāyatanādikaṃdukavṛttiyopena rakṣeta saḥ ||  
  
yaḥ śrīdharmaśivaḥ prabhu vabhayākrandaikahetukṛtīkarttā   
bhūrikavīndrakarṇakanakānekapravandhātmanāṃ |   
tacchiṣyo vimalaḥ śivondhayavanaiḥ śrīrājyapālādibhiḥ |   
khātaiḥ | sadguṇacāribhiḥ kṛtanatirddīkṣāmavādimāṃ ||  
  
117b)  
  
vimalāvatyāṃ dīkṣāvidhiḥ pañcamaḥ || grantha 800 ||  
  
  
līlaṃ yasmin samastaṃ kṣitijaladahanāt pūrvaśaktṛstakāryaṃ |   
kalpānte tatvasarge punarapi bhuvanādyogataṃ tadyatā bhūt |   
  
talliṅgaśaścadā ||  
  
dyaṃnirūpamamamalamukhyagauṇāti gauṇaṃ |   
natvāvrūte pratiṣṭhāṃ harasikharitarūbhoganirvāṇa hetu ||  
  
mukhyaṃ liṅgamanālamba nityoditamakhaṇḍitaṃ |  
gauṇaṃ nādasvarūpaṃ syādati gauṇaṃ śadāśivaḥ ||  
  
vyaktisthāna tayā bhaktestacchando'śmābhi nirmite |   
vyaktāvyakte bhayākāre vāṇarohādikeṣvapi ||   
  
vyaktaṃ spaṣṭaśiro grīvā mukhadyujjaghaṇāntikaṃ |  
avyaktaṃ catuṣṭāśravṛttabhāgopalakṣitaṃ ||   
  
vyaktāvyaktaṃ catustryeka mukhapaṃkaja bhūṣaṇaṃ |  
devaḥ sadāśivo vāṇo vāṇo vāṇo suropi ca ||  
  
tena tasmai kṛtaṃ yasmād vāṇaliṅgantataḥ smṛtaṃ |  
  
118a)  
  
svayaṃ bhūliṅgavadvāḥṇaliṅga bhuktyai ca muktaye ||  
  
sahasraguṇamanyasmānnate sthāpana pūjanāt |  
phalaṃ vānādi liṅgānā proktaṃ liṅgārṇave vahuḥ ||  
  
ye nyonyan pṛṣṭhapāśāṇa rauhāsta sarvasiddhidā |  
kathitā pūjanīyāśca nadīpraśravaṇodbhavaḥ ||  
  
putrāṇāyuśriyo bhṛtyānyaccānyanmanasepsitaṃ |  
sphāṭikaliṅgamāsādya yajamānaḥ samasnute ||  
  
liṅgavitānasṛṣṭiḥ syāt siddhimuktī dhanāni vā |  
vāhyaṃ vā bhṛbhṛtāyasmāt tasmālliṅgārcanaṃ caraṃ ||  
  
ādityā vaśavo rudrā viśve devāstathāśvinau |  
vidhivalliṅgamārādhya padamiṣṭatamaṃ gatāḥ ||  
  
mṛdbhasmago sakṛt piṣṭaguḍekhaścādi nirmitaṃ |  
saṃpūjayet pratiṣṭhārtha śraddhāvāṇadhi gacchati ||  
  
sailamṛddārumallāharameścitrā visambhavaḥ |  
kṛtāstha kidhiyalliṅgamabhīṣṭaṃ phaladaṃ bhavet ||  
  
liṅgasya dakṣiṇā tasya śate pūjitaḥ | sthāpanādapi | uttare ||  
  
118b)  
  
ttaraḥ | śreṣṭaphalaṃ muktaṃ hi dehināṃ |   
pāda pratiṣṭhā mukhyā ca dvārasya hṛdayasya ca? |   
samudāyāṣṭajasyeti pratiṣṭhā pañcadhā smṛtāḥ ||   
  
arghadānādikaṃ yattatraivāttargatirbhavet |  
kriyāśaktyātmakaṃ pīṭhaṃ rodhaśaktyātmana prabhoḥ ||  
  
adhiṣṭeyaṃtayoryāgā yo mantrabhāvanānvitaṃḥ |  
dṛkkriyā *? sthā pratiṣṭhā vidhiryukteśvarārjane ||  
  
vidhiṣṭamūttau vidhivat sannidhānaṃ viśeṣataḥ |   
parasya vyāpino yatsā pratiṣṭhādiṣu ||  
  
so pratiṣṭhā tu yasyaudbrahmaśilādayojanāt |  
tatsthāpanaṃ yatra pīṭhe nyāsau vāṇādi vadvidhau ||  
  
pāṭhakānāñca mahatāṃ sthita sthāpanaṃ |  
pratimālokaliṅgānāṃsāsthāpanaśatakratau ||  
  
utthāpane syājjirṇādya dvārayuktaṃ kumārake |  
  
ittha pañcadhāthātaḥ | kathyate bhūparitrahaḥ |   
  
viprādīnāṃ mahī raktapītā camevakāḥ |  
sarpiśoṇita gomūtra surāgandhāhitā kramāt ||  
  
darbhaṃ śarā śakāśa yuktā susvanisālitī |  
  
119a)  
  
iṣṭavarṇādyabhāvepi varṇādyāpādanaṃ caret |  
prāgīśa saumya sarvatra plavāgurvī dṛḍhāsatāṃ ||  
  
yathāhastasite khāte pūrṇe'bhṛmṛttikā'dhekā |  
sāsuśreṣṭhādharitrī syājalārvā parīkṣitāḥ ||  
  
atīvaśodhayetbhūmimasthyaṃgārādadūṣitāṃ |  
vahudhā karṣaṇaiḥ khātairgokulādiliveśanaiḥ ||  
  
nadī pūrvavahā yatra valmīka vālakāvilaiḥ |  
yuktāsyā *? kravyādapaśupakṣantajāśrayoḥ ||  
  
hemahālaiḥ śatotkṛṣṭā tatrāccontetilāndhayet |  
ato vaktavya vidhinā yāgadhānādike kṛte ||  
  
kramādvārādi vahnī sa pūjātṛptyavaśāni kīṃ |  
kriyāṃ niṣpādya juhuyādahorātraṃ sahaśrakaṃ ||  
  
samāyāṃ copaliptāyāṃ disaḥ saṃśodhayedbhuviḥ |  
vāstuṃ kṛtvādadedreṣāṃ pradakṣāṃmamutādināṃ ||  
  
madhyādīśānakoṣṭhasthaṃ saṃpūrṇaṃ kalaśaṃ yajet |  
śivavadathavāstuṃ ca saṃmyaksiṃcecca tajjālaiḥ ||  
  
119b)  
  
kuṣvālādi tato bāhya bhyarcya rakṣo grahākṣiret |  
daśadikṣu paścāpaścāsi kṣoṇīñca pūjayet ||  
  
hyuddālādi tathā hyasya paṭe pūjāṃ tu khānayet |  
madhu pṛkta kundālune svabhiśiktena deśintaḥ ||  
  
magnikoṣṭaṃ kṣipedrakṣo diśimṛtsvāṃśanaistataḥ |  
kumbhāmbho nikṣipedgarte siṃcccecca sarvato mahīṃ ||  
  
dvitīyakumbhavastrādi cchannaṃ vipreṇa grāhayet |  
prācyāṃ sthitvā kṣaṇaṃ cihna śilāḥ siñcanmyaṭāmbubhiḥ ||  
  
pradakṣiṇaṃ yāvadīśa koṇaṃ kumbha bhramāditi |  
parigrahārtha dānena bhuvaḥ syājjanasākṣikaṃ ||  
  
vāstumiṣṭvāśivakumbhe tadvaktrage ghṛtaiḥ |  
pūrṇe śarāve svetādi vartyādīpa catuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
tatvātat sthiti nāśābhyāṃ diśedvarṇo nandayānayau |  
samahīnādhikaṃ vāpi pūrvadhāmādi rodhakaṃ ||  
  
kurvanmṛtkamavāpnoti prāśādādyañca daivataḥ |  
ubhayo dvigunocchāyaṃ nāhaṃ nyatkṣānayoḥ kramāt ||  
  
120a)  
  
tatpādañca puraḥ pṛṣṭhe pārśvayo kha hramādikaṃ |  
bhinnanābhau kramanveśa nābhinna vāṇabhāṣaṇāt ||  
  
jalāntaṃ karkarāntaṃ vā prāśādārthaṃ tu śodhayet |  
ājānu vāṇaliṅgaṃ vā prāsāda khamakhātake ||  
  
gṛhe bhū gavasata cinmātraṃ vātadarddhakaṃ |  
mukhabhṛnnābhi guhyāntaṃ jānuṃ taṃ cātmaśaktitaḥ ||  
  
yāvadvā bhūmiśuddhisyāccandroktṛmācamatādivit |  
dhāmārtha metadapyuktaṃ vṛhadvirodhanādiṣu ||  
  
piṅgaloktānunā kartṛṃ śilyācārpyādi varmaṇi |  
sūtrapātakratau vāpi svajasvakādi niveśanaiḥ ||  
  
praśvevakādi varmaiśca sujñānaṃ prathayaṃjane |  
śabdairkaṇḍūyanairyannairnirvikāṇatā kvacit ||  
  
yannāma yatnataṃ spṛsya śṛṇuyādyantadātmakaṃ |  
samīpe prāntato madhye digmātramidamīritaṃ ||  
  
cidrumaṃ hemago śṛṅgo muktāratnamaṇirdhanaṃ |  
najataṃ saṅkhaśuktīñca bhe *? ku mṛtāmṛtau ||  
  
tatraucāropayedbhṛyaḥ sarvadā sarvasiddhaye |  
  
120b)  
  
liptagarta bhuvau vāstu devāniṣṭāsaśatkuśaiḥ |  
kṣmāmulikhyābhirāśicya tathā gandhavadambubhiḥ ||  
  
vedāśravisvesmākārāṃ bhūṣitāṃ pṛthivīṃ yajet |  
khātapādo namāpūro kṛtamaṇḍapa śaktiyaḥ ||  
  
mantra tṛpto yajñaḥ | ṣṭogacchetaṃ snānamaṇḍapaṃ ||  
  
dharmādi saṃjñakāḥ pādāḥ śilāḥ prāsāda liṅgānāḥ |  
vitastimātrā vedāgrāskuryāṃgulocchritā dṛḍhāḥ ||  
  
aiṣṭaskai eṣṭakaidhāsniśailaśailyai vasūcchrayā |  
hastamānānavapadātadavajrādi(?) ciṃhnitāḥ ||  
  
pañca padmai svastikairvā sarvā eva samāstataḥ |  
karadīrghārddha vistārā aṣṭāṅgulocchritā madhyeṃ ||  
  
gṛhepi pañca navavāyathā sobhañca dāruje |  
nandā bhadrā jayā pūrṇāpyajitā vā parājitā ||  
  
vijayāmaṅgalāndhanyā dharaṇī vāstva mānavaḥ |  
subhadrotha vibhadrākhyaḥ sunanda puṣpadantakaḥ ||  
  
jayo vijayanāmā ca kumbhapūrvāstathottaraḥ |  
savasunidhikumbhoḥ syuḥ pañcānāpañca tadyathā ||  
  
121a)  
  
nandābhadrājayāraktā pūrṇānāṃ vimalotkaṭe |  
padmomahāpadmaśākṣomarakatamumudrakau ||  
  
saṃsnāpya vācyavatsarvā liptāvastrāvṛtāḥ śilāḥ |  
yāgauka śiśu śayyāyāṃ dābhyāṃ vāpi niveśayet ||  
  
yatacchāsanake puṣpaṃ candanādiṣu carcitāḥ |  
hṛtānāsunyeśedvyādi kṣmāntatatvaṃ svasajñayā ||  
  
ūrddhamadhyeyyadho bhāge śilānāmuṣṭiterpite |  
śivavidyātma tatve tu mūrtīstandhoparinyaśet ||  
  
tadūrddhe mūrtipāśceṣṭā navavā pañcacānyayat |  
sannidhāya sannirūpya śmared khaṇḍa trayaṃ kramāt ||  
  
ma *? di svānta paryantaṃ manastasmātrakāvadhiḥ |  
hayātrādi mahīprāntaṃ śivavidyātmanā padaṃ ||  
  
sarvakarmakhabhyānta vā tritatvaṃ jyānapuñjake |  
yadvā madhya śilāyāṃ syāt sarvanyāso parāsvapi ||  
  
aikekamūrtisaṃyogastatvadhyā * di pūrvavat |  
prācina tatva saṃtṛpti śu'ddhisparśa japādikaṃ ||  
  
tatva trayepi kurvīta paścādratnādi saṃyutān |  
  
121b)  
  
pūrṇānājyena madhunā pañcagavyārtha sevitān |  
tāmrakumbhāt samabhyarcya diśādhīśādhi devatān ||  
  
vidadhyāt sannidhau teṣā homasvasvāmibhiḥ kramāt |  
śilānāmapi sarvāṣāṃ cintayedadhi devatāḥ ||  
  
śmerāsyāḥ śuddhasvarṇābhā vidyārūpādhṛtā plavāḥ |  
nānālaṅkāracāccaṅgī tato vāstvādi śuddhaye ||  
  
śataṃṣārddhādi mūlena pūrṇānta vāśinā hunet |  
sūtrayitvā devakulaṃ vāsto viśvaṃ vivartayet ||  
  
aṣṭāṣṭakoṣṭhakaiḥ prāgvaccatuḥpadalidaṃ likhet |  
datvā koṇeṣu vaṃsau dvādaṣṭau rajurvikoṇataḥ ||  
  
dvipadā ṣaṭpadāstāśca tatra vāstuṃ yajed yathā |  
pūjānāmapacāreṇa cākṣuṣasyāntare manāḥ ||  
  
tamo mayamabhūghoraṃ bhūtamatyadbhutaṃ kilaḥ |  
vaṃsāṃbhyāṃ rajjubhigāḍhantaṃ saṃyamyāmarā sthitāḥ ||  
  
taddehe hyāṇavāhinyau nyautryānyā nandikeśvare |  
uttānamasurākāra mārgacetatanūrudaṃ ||  
  
122a)  
  
pūjāyāṃ cintayed vāstumathajaghe niveśanaiḥ |  
adhomukhantathāvastatanūrddhā bhūṣitaḥ pumān ||  
  
brahmaṇābhiḥ sa pindapādīśamūrddhāpavaktakathatadvatsakandharaḥ |  
koṇayugmabhṛtyāṇi yugmakaḥ |  
  
ditiparjyanyaśabdārthau jayāditya sa yugmakaḥ |  
samīndrādi bhujorakṣo digsayugmeṣa yugmakaḥ ||  
  
mitro viṣasvāntasyāruṣāmadakṣiṇa saṃjñakaiḥ |  
rogapūśau ca jānūdvau marīcyavaṇibhṛtstataḥ ||  
  
jaghavitathaśoṣādyā evaṃ vāstu hitorcitaḥ |  
madhyaścatuspade brahmā marīcī prāci ṣaṭpade ||  
  
sāvitrī sūryavṛrdhādho dvi koṣṭha vahni koṣṭhage |  
antakaḥ ṣaṭpado yāmya indropendrī pade pade ||  
  
nai-ṛtyāmathapaṅkastho valabhadrastu paścime |  
rudraśca kārtike paśca vāyau koṣṭha dvaye tataḥ ||  
  
uttare ṣaṭpado meruriśe hi malayopyuma |  
aiṣa padārddhatvīśānaḥ parjanyaḥ kāśyapaḥ pade ||  
  
indraśca savitā dharmaḥ kāmaśca prāgdiśi sthitaḥ |  
  
122b)  
  
ākāśāgnī vahnikoṇe padāddhapadagāminau |  
pūṣādharmāṅgārakaśca yamonāradabhṛṅginau ||  
  
yāmyapaṃktau tato rakṣaḥ koṣṭhārddha mṛga āhvavaṃ |  
aparārddhe ca piṇḍañca śālaṅkāyana kīrtanāt ||  
  
athanandī mahārka * *? garuḍoraruṇaḥ pade |  
rāhuḥ śanaiścaraḥ pratyagdiśivāyau ca pūrvavat ||  
  
kaituvāyu saumya pakṣau vāsaki viśvakarmaṇā |  
nārddhaṃ kuverasa *? ścānantādibhyoditi jalai ||  
  
īśāvyarakī vidārī putanāpāparākṣaśī |  
proktaskandoryamājambhaḥ pilipicchaśca diksthitāḥ ||  
  
ityarcā vāsturvāstvāpi haviṣyairnāma vādibhiḥ |  
asaṃpūjyasurānetāstiryañcāśacca vāstugān ||  
  
yaḥ kariṣyati sāmādyamāsurantadvirodha kṛt |  
ato vāstu sthitāṃ devāṃ kramāt sampūjya śraddhayā ||  
  
punyāheṣvapi sarveṣu kuryāt karmāparantataḥ |  
sthiravāsturiti proktaṃ ścarāpyatha kvacidyathā ||  
  
123a)  
  
bhādrādimāsaprāgmūrddhāmārgādau yāmyamastakaḥ |  
pratyaksirāḥ phālgunādau jyeṣṭhādau saumyako hi rāṭ ||  
  
vāmāṅga sāyinastasya kroḍe kroḍa mukha gṛhaṃ |  
anyathā naiva kartavyaṃ mātmanasubhamicchatāḥ ||  
  
ekāśīti padairvāstuṅgṛhārthamathavartayet |  
tripadā ṣaṭpadā tatra rajjayo navakoṣṭhasau ||  
  
dvau vaṃsau madhyagau brahmā bhavennava padaḥ sadāḥ |  
marīcyādyāḥ ṣaṭpadasthā āpādyāśca dvikoṣṭhagāḥ ||  
  
iśādyā padikāḥ sarve carakpādyāśca vākyataḥ |  
catuṣaṣṭhi padaiḥ sarva vaikāśīlyāśurārayaḥ ||  
  
yajeddurga purāṭgāra nagaragrāmakheṭake |  
śayyāśana vimāneṣu calācala gṛheṣu ca ||  
  
siddhi sthāne maṭhe harma yāgādau kha hramādiṣu |  
vāpīkūpataḍāgādau vanaco *? nramādiṣu ||  
  
ūktānukteṣu sarveṣu vāstu śata padaṃ tadā |  
brahmādyāsuradhāmoktyā bhāgāccandrādayastathā ||  
  
rāyuśīśca grahānbhūta *? dakoṣṭaiḥ prapūjayet |  
yajedbhityādiṣu sadā mahāmarpyāṇi dvādaśaḥ ||  
  
123b)  
  
vajrādīnyathavāṃ sarvaṃ kṣetraṃ yatsā *? yedvahiḥ |  
athāhuti trayandatvā pratideva yathākramaṃ ||  
  
bhūtebhyo valimāhṛtya śubhalagne śilānyaset |  
madhyagarte nyaśecchaktiṃ kumbhañcānanta saṃjñakaṃ ||  
  
lavarṇārūḍhamūlena tatraiva dharaṇīśilāṃ |  
svatantrādīnghaṭāvaṣṭau kāṣṭāsvaityādiṣu kramāt ||  
  
nyastaśaktiṣu subhreṣu śakrādi mantraninyaset |  
lūkamādyai mūrtipāṇāṃ rāṣinandādikāśilāḥ ||  
  
palādāropayet teṣu yathāsyābhitti madhyagāḥ |  
vidiśāsudiśāṣuṣṭhau tāsudharmādikānapi ||  
  
subhadrādyeṣu nandādyāścatamrāgnyādito matāḥ |  
ajitādyāśca prāgādi jayādi sveva satkṛtāḥ ||  
  
brahmāṇaṃ coparinyasya vyāpinañca maheśvaraṃ |  
bhāvayedeṣyamadhvānaṃ vyomaprāsādamadhyagaṃ ||  
  
bhūyo bhūtavaliṃ datvā śastravighnaṃ haraṃ yajet |  
śilāpañcaka pakṣepi samudrakalaśopari ||  
  
nyaśet pūrṇāśilāṃ madhyenyādikoṇeṣvanu kramāt |  
padmādiṣvevanandādyāḥ syuḥ svayaṃ tvādiṣu nathaḥ ||  
  
madhyā bhāvāścataśroṣi mātṛsadbhāva kīrtitāḥ |  
oṃ pūrṇetvaṃ mahāvidye sarvasaṃdohalakṣaṇe ||  
  
sarvasaṃpūrṇamevātra kuruṣvāyi rasaḥ kramāt |  
oṃ nandanandinī yugmāṃ tvāmatrasthāpayāmyahaṃ ||  
  
prāsāde tiṣṭhasaṃhṛṣṭā yāvaccandrārka tārakaṃ |  
āyuḥ kāmaṃ śriyaṃ nandendehi vāsiṣṭi dehināṃ ||  
  
tasmitrakṣā sadākāryā prāsāde yatnatastvayā |  
oṃ bhadre sarvadā bhadraṃ lokānāṃ kurukāśyapi ||  
  
āyurdākāmadevi śrīpadā ca sadā bhavaṃ |  
oṃ jayatra sadādevi tiṣṭhatvaṃ sthāpitā mayā ||  
  
nityaṃ jayāyabhūtyai ca svāminā bhava bhārgavai |  
oṃ rikte riktadoṣaghnasiddhimukti prade śubhe ||  
  
sarvadā sarvadeśastha tiṣṭhāśminniśarūpini |  
dakṣiṇāṃ sarvayāgeṣu gṛhītvā visṛjet kratuṃ ||  
  
pūrayitvā dṛḍhaṃ khātaṃ pīṭhabandhamathā caret |  
  
124b)  
  
tatrāpi vāstu sampūjye jaghodya vinivedyayet ||  
  
śilānyāśaḥ ||  
  
atha devapratiṣṭhaupayogikālādigadyate |  
tatra muktau sarvadevamuktyau devajña sādhite ||  
  
caragnādau tadādyarthamudagmārga gate ravau |  
dakṣiṇe svayane pūjyaṃ trivarśorddha bhayāvahaṃ ||  
  
ādau kiñcit subhaṃ kṛtvā paścād mukhāvaha bhavet |  
rāhugrastarka indrau vācyādibhiḥ pīḍyate prajāḥ ||  
  
kumāro sa prapīḍyante kanyānāśaṅkāyante |  
sumahāndhasukopaśca bhūrbhujāṃ jāyate tathā ||  
  
kartakṣayaḥ sadāśoko gṛhe bhavati dāruṇaḥ |  
śubhārcane pravatteta umāgaṅge svaroktitaḥ ||  
  
kāraṇa tritaye cādya śurāśuragurudaye |  
ariktāsti peyo ṣaṣṭhyā nindyavārāditojjhitāḥ ||  
  
dhaniṣṭhārdrāśatabhiṣāśravaṇa cottarātrayaṃ |  
rohiṇī cānurādheti sthirārambhāmahodayā ||  
  
lalagnañca siṃhako daṇḍa vṛṣakanyātulā ghaṭā |  
vṛścikaścaiti sūśreṣṭhātāniśrīsundare yathā ||  
  
125a)  
  
pūrvāṣāḍho turāśāḍhā hastāpuṣpā ca śahiṇī |  
viprasyaitāni śastāni punarvasūdhaniṣṭhayā ||  
  
citrā ca śravaṇāṃrājña uttarā cādre raivatīṃ |  
aśvinī ceti vaiśyasya svātīśaṃpūrvaphālgunī ||  
  
maghā vā varavarṇasya sāmānyo tatva sekhare |  
maṇḍapastvagrataḥ kāryaḥ styaktvā pañcāṅgulā mahīṃ ||  
  
dhāmno dhāmāntaraṃ vāpi śopānāddaśavākarān |  
ekādirandhra hastānta liṅgānāṃ dvidvivṛddhitaḥ ||  
  
digdvādaśādito yāva ṣaṭviṃśa cāṣṭaviṃśati |  
prāgvadarddhaḥ snānārthaṃ vedī yānvito vidhau ||  
  
dvitricatuskaraistatra vedhau hīnāhitaḥ sa ca |  
ekatoraṇa aindrāsyaścaturddhāstoraṇopi vā ||  
  
īśāne prāvisaumye vā syātmakhyaṃ maṇḍapopivā |  
ekadvitri kare liṅge vasvakaṃ paṃkti saṃmitāḥ ||  
  
maṇḍapāścaturhastā dedvidvivṛdvyā bhavanti vā |  
ghanoghoro virājo'rtha kāṃcanaḥ kāmarāmakau ||  
  
125b)  
  
suveśorghaṃrpyarodakṣo nāmānye ādadhīcake |  
liṅgānāñca narādrāṇāṃ sāntarāṇāṃ karāditaḥ ||  
  
ekādaśakarā dvi dvi vṛddhyāḥ syuḥ saptaviṃśatiḥ |  
vāṇeroheramyajādau sudiptāskarauthavā ||  
  
dvāraucchrayāntaraṃ tyaktvā gṛhaliṅge gṛhāgrataḥ |  
japāṣoḍaśahastaḥ syāt maṇḍapaḥ piṅgalāmate ||  
  
vipulo vibhramo bhūrirmahāhīmaṇḍapāstrayaḥ |  
pañcāśadoditaḥ pañca pañca hastairvinā kvacit ||  
  
candrāgnīdvarcimānbhūtakāraibhyūrmaṇḍapāstrayaḥ |  
mahārddhānā kulahīna madhyamottama bhedataḥ ||  
  
śreṣṭaṃ vāmādi hīnesyānotumedhamakalpanāḥ |  
yathāśoḍaṣa hastasyātmaṇḍapaḥ sarvakarmaṣu ||  
  
adhivāsamaṇḍapārthā pracchannādvicchadā kuṭī |  
upaskarārthaṃ pūrvāsyā vāruṇyāṃ rakṣitā bhavet ||  
  
mūlamaṇḍape tulyā vā maṇḍalārthaṃ tu maṇḍapaḥ |  
daśāṣṭasaṅkaro cchedā jyeṣṭādestilakoktitaḥ ||  
  
126a)  
  
vidheyā maṇḍapā tulyasustambhaṃ toraṇāditau |  
vistārārkāṃ śataḥ kuryādaiṣṭakīmupajaghintāḥ ||  
  
ūrddheścatuṣkikāt pañca paṭalai ṣaṭbhirācitaṃ |  
dṛḍhācchidrena caivaṃśa vṛkṣa'śākhādiśaissaśaiḥ ||  
  
sthūṇāścatasrakoṇeṣu dve dve dvāreṣu pārśvayoḥ |  
aparāśca yathāśobha dvihastādiṣutāmatāḥ ||  
  
madhye catuṣkarā vedī koṇastambhaścatuṣṭayaṃ |  
aṣṭāṅgulocchrayānmeṣāṃ hastāṅguṣṭaika varjitāḥ ||  
  
vistarāccocchrayāt pādaṃ varddhayet sāntareṣvapi |  
maṇḍapanavadhā hṛkte vedī madhya padena tu ||  
  
kuṇḍānāṃ vistaraḥ śeṣaḥ yarddhāvedīpitā maha |  
liṅgāyāmadvivistārāścaturaśro samantataḥ ||  
  
hastādūrddhaṃṣkacidvedī ṣaṣṭhaḍaṅgula varddhitāḥ |  
vedī pādāntaraṃ tyaktvā kuṇḍāni navapañca ca ||  
  
trīṇī naidrāpyatonekaṃ prāgmapyāgnīśānyataraḥ śuroḥ |  
avyaktasthāpane kuṇḍaṃ vṛttaṃ sarvāsu dikṣu ca ||  
  
bhuktau muktau tadā puṣṭau jīrṇe dvāro viśeṣataḥ |  
  
126b)  
  
vyakte yugāśramaṣṭāśravyaktāvyakte śrivartanaḥ |  
digvidikṣunyaśetyaccamathādimadavarjitaḥ ||  
  
vedāśraṃ yoni khaṇḍendu tryaśraṃ vṛttaṣaḍaśrakaṃ |  
padmamaṣṭāṃ sametāni prāgādīśāntamarpayet ||  
  
sāmrākṣe śatrusantāpe māraṇe vyādhvakopane |  
āyuḥ śrīṣuṣṭapai dhairya cāṭe śrībuddhipuṣṭaye ||  
  
sarvakāmāptaye caitā nyuktāni diksvanu kramāt |  
pūrvaṣa madhyato jñeyannavamaṃ pūrvavat sthitaṃ ||  
  
vedāśrārddhaṃ tu vṛttābjāṣṭaśrāṇi dikṣu veṣataḥ |  
caturaśrāṇiṃ sarvāṇi vṛttāni kathitāni vā ||  
  
hasto nihastake nyāni sāṅgāni dvi dvi buddhitaḥ |  
bhānuṃreṇḍaṃtacaṃlikhyā pūkācaṃ yavamaṣṭadhā ||  
  
guṇitaṃ hyaṃgulaṃ śreṣṭaṃ madhyaṃ hīnaṃ surairaśaiḥ |  
daśatvaṃ guṇiparvāṇi prādeśaśavarīśvare ||  
  
aṅguṣṭhasya pradeśinyā vyāśaprādeśa ānalau |  
tālauruṇe madhyamāyāśaukarṇaścāpya nāmayā ||  
  
127a)  
  
jalaḥ śivāgamādau tu vitastauparibhāvitaḥ |  
kaniṣṭhayā vitastistu dvādaśāṅgula aiṣṭike ||  
  
catuviṃśāṅgulau hastastu rantireka viṃśati |  
kiṣṇurdakṣedvyarannirvāṇalvakiṣṇu catucatuḥ śataḥ ||  
  
caturhastādhanurdaṇḍo nālikāyugayugmakaṃ |  
dhanu sahaśre dvekośo gavyatadviguṇaṃ yame ||  
  
aṣṭau dhanusahaśrāṇi yojanaṃ koṣalāmate |  
ṣaṭsaptāṣṭayavaistirya smṛtasthairvā tu śātuṣaiḥ ||  
  
hīna madhyottamānisyumāne trīnyaṅgulāni tustilairyavo vāṣṭa   
yavairaṅgulamuttamaṃ |  
  
yajamānātmahastaṃ vā caturviṃśati vā bhajet |  
caturaṅgula yukto vā svīya hasto yathāsthitaḥ ||  
  
jyeṣṭhāṅguṣṭhaścaturviṃśa saṃkhyā vāhaye śīrṣake |  
kuvvītasusamaṃ kuṇḍaṃ tiryagūrddhasamekhalaṃ ||  
  
śrīskanda vijayādyeṣu tvanyathā na tu darśanaṃ |  
ekāṅgulo vahiḥ kaṇṭhodyaṅgulo vāmataṅgake ||  
  
kuṇḍākārāmekhalāsyā tiryagūrddhaṃ ca sāsamā |  
prāgvadvitryarvāyuraśaircāgulai pañcatā kramāt ||  
  
127b)  
  
mekhalāmakhyato nābhiḥ kuṇḍārddhātryaṅgavistarāḥ |  
mūlontagranisnālyādaṃ gulaikocchrayādharā ||  
  
dyucchritā vā svastha patra sadṛśyaṅguṣṭhaṃ mekhalāḥ |  
arddhāvadhitatodhatvāt kramaśoddhāṃgulā bhavet ||  
  
yonikuṇḍākṛti vai tanmadhye lakṣmaikamaṅgulaṃ |  
prāgvahyāṃtakakuṇḍānāṃ nābhiḥ saumyā nanāmatāḥ ||  
  
śeṣānāṃ prāgmukhīśāna dikkuṇḍe nyatamātayoḥ |  
kuṇḍaṃ sūryāṅgulaṃ paṃcaviṃśamātraṃ trimekhalaṃ ||  
  
śatārddhamuṣṭihastākhyaṃ śateranti sahaśrake |  
hastaṃ vāvayute lakte caturo niyate tu ṣaṭ ||  
  
aṣṭahastaṃ koṭi homepyata ūrddhaṃ na kārayet |  
raṃ praṃtvagni pavairarkāṃgulaimuṣṭau tathāṅgulaiḥ ||  
  
dvekāddhairalau tridvekairhastai'vyagniyamaistrayaṃ |  
dvikareṣadvatūrāmaisturyākhya'ṣṭaṣadvibhiḥ ||  
  
rudrāṣṭaṣaḍbhiḥ saṭvāsta'pyaṣṭamerkadigaṣṭabhiḥ |  
pañcaikā vā mekhalaiṣṭāṃ yoniśca hāstike yathā ||  
  
128a)  
  
dvyaṅgulādvyaṅgulāvṛddhi vistārayāmato'thavā |  
aindrādi mantra kuṇḍāni noktāni vistaratvataḥ ||  
  
vaṭodumvara bodhibhru pūjāstāraṇa mūrtayeḥ |  
plakṣodumbarakāśvastha vaṭā prāgāditopi cā ||  
  
eṣāmekatamadgrāhyamabhāvena tu sampadi |  
nyagrodhaśca palāśaśco dumbaropyatha siddhakaḥ ||  
  
aśvattha vāpimādhūka pūjyā bilva iti kramāt |  
aṣṭadvāreṣu nirdiṣṭāḥ sārdrāḥ saṃtāraṇā api ||  
  
prāgīśa vahni koṇeṣu dvāraṃ pūrvānanaṃ trayaṃ |  
paścime nair-ṛte vāyau tritaya pratyagāsyakaṃ ||  
  
uttare pyuttaramukhaṃ dakṣa vaktraṃ ca dakṣiṇe |  
vaśvagrāśca turaśrā vā vṛttā sarvepi toraṇāḥ ||  
  
pañcapaṭsaptahastāsta kanyaśānāṃ bhavantite |  
madhyamānāñca jyeṣṭhānāmaṣṭaṣṭyaṅgulavṛtaḥ ||  
  
kanīyasā toraṇāṇāṃ khāto hastapramāṇakaḥ |  
trayāṇāṃ madhyasaṃsthānāṃ vedāṅgula vivaddhritaḥ ||  
  
khātaḥ sārddhakarojñeya tuttamādi trayasya tu |  
kāpyaśau pañcamāśena bhūmi *? vasena vā ||  
  
128b)  
  
śākhāyāṃrantaraṃgulyamucchrāyenorddhatopi vā |  
syasvayorvā lalāṭasya vāhulyaṃ syāt saḍaṅgulaṃ ||  
  
pañcahastapramenyatra vṛddhidvyekāṅgulāthavā |  
śalyamaṣṭāṅgulaṃ hāstena cānte ṣoḍaśāṅgulaṃ ||  
  
tatpakṣa *? laśṛṅgāni vistṛtiḥ pañcamāṃśataḥ |  
dvyaṅgulaṃ cāsya praveśyamekāṅgulottaraṃ kramāt ||  
  
madhye śrīḥ svastikaṃ padma cotpalaṃ lakṣmikeśave |  
dhārikāstoraṇestulyā vedīṣuṣṭāsudunnatāḥ ||  
  
dvāreṣu kadalīsveṣṭā ghaṭāśca sayavārakāḥ |  
brahmāsadviguṇaṃ pīṭhaṃ vistārāṃ kṣīravṛkṣajaṃ ||  
  
catuṣpādaṃ sarojāṅka mucchrayoṣṭāḍaśāṃṅgulaṃ |  
yadivotu samucchedhaṃ dviguṇaṃ vistareṇa ca ||  
  
kanyaśānāṃ bhadraṃ pīṭhaṃ vistarā dviguṇaṃ kvacit |  
anukrameṇa cānyeṣāṃ caturaṅgula vṛddhitaḥ ||  
  
navānāṃ trīṇi pīṭhāni proktāni rauravoture |  
patākāḥ saptahastāḥ syuḥ dhvajāḥ pañcantarāstathā ||  
  
viṃśatyaṅgulavistārā navaśadvastra nirmitāḥ |  
  
129a)  
  
jyeṣṭhāditonasvaiḥ paṃktyā munibhivāmatādhvajāḥ |  
hastadvitaya vistārā yadvā śreṣṭeṣu hastakāḥ ||  
  
karadvitayavistārā arddhahāni kramāttataḥ |  
hastamātra pravistārāḥ patākāḥ sa dhvajāḥ sthitāḥ ||  
  
kvaciddvihastadīrghāsyuḥ karamātra pravistarāḥ |  
pītāśakrāyudhā bhāvā prācyā dhvajāpatākikā ||  
  
dhūmrāgaurāgni varṇā āgneyyāṃ nāradeśvare |  
dakṣiṇādhūṣarā kṛṣṇā yadvādhūmanibhāḥ śubhāḥ ||  
  
nai-ṛtepi śuvarṇābhā nīlākṛṣṇā sudhūṣadāḥ |  
vāruṇe pāṇḍarā svetāḥ raktāvādyanasaṃnibhāḥ ||  
  
gaurāvāharitā vāyau pītaḥ soṇāstathottare |  
śitāvāṃvudasaṃkāśā iśāne devi yāmale ||  
  
tatreva brahmaṇo raktā nīlā ca nai-ṛte hare |  
madhye svetā vicitrā vā devyāmatādi mūditāḥ ||  
  
sāntau sarvepi susvetāḥ saubhāgyai hiṅgulopamāḥ |  
haridrābhāśubhaṃ nasyu māraṇe kajjalopamāḥ ||  
  
daṇḍāḥ kara praviṣṭāsyu dhvajānāṃ paṃca hastakāḥ |  
  
129b)  
  
daśahastāpatākānā pañcamātme praveśitā |  
cūtapallavadāmādi yathā sobhañca vinyaset ||  
  
athā bhyantaratastasmādvastaiścūrṇairvilepanaiḥ |  
virtānaṃ maṇḍapāntasyā vedikoparidhā kvacit ||  
  
vṛttātsānti ghaṭān kuṇḍaṃ saṃkhyayā nyonyapi nyaset |  
mūrdhni nidrā ghaṭobhūṣī śivamkumbhāstrarvarddhanī ||  
  
suyovināśarāvena saṃyuktāni vraṇādinā |  
pañcāśāṅgulavāhalya śaptaviṃśāṅgulacchritaḥ ||  
  
aṣṭāṅgulamukhaṃ kumbhā navatyaṃgula veṣṭanaḥ |  
etacchaṣṭāṃśahīnopi varddhinī vatrunālikā ||  
  
dvayaṃ vāpi yathāśobhaṃ dṛḍhaṃ na sphuṭādikāṃ |  
vedāṅgulocchritāṣṭābhirāyatāra sa vistṛtāḥ ||  
  
praṇītāyasanāhāṣṭadīrghadaṇḍācyutārcane |  
yadvā pañcaucchitāṣṭābhirvistṛtādvādaśāyatāḥ ||  
  
prāgvadaṇḍayutākāryā vāmadevemahattadā |  
dvevāṇanāhartu dīrghadaṇḍe vā kulasaṃskṛtau ||  
  
camasasyāṃvu pūrṇasya daṇḍapaścimatohitaḥ |  
  
130a)  
  
caturaśraṃ tathākhātaṃ yathāśobhaṃ vṛhanmaye |  
aninditā samacchadā samidho yajñavṛkṣajāḥ ||  
  
na kaniṣṭā'pi kāsthaulye ṛdhyaprādeśasaṃmitāḥ |  
arkaḥ palāśa khadirā vapāmārgāthapipyalaḥ ||  
  
udumbarasamīdūrvā kuśāsūryādiśāntaye |  
aṣṭādhikaṃ śataṃ daiyāmarddhaṃ vā saptaviṃśati ||  
  
aṣṭāviṃśati yāgrāhyaṃ pratyekaṃ nyūnameva vā |  
kuśāḥ śaddeśajāḥ snigdhāḥ nāti khavvāna vāyatāḥ ||  
  
śukacchāyā sāgramūlāḥ saptaparṇā na saptajāḥ |  
pathijāthaścitā jātaḥ smaśānepi tṛtarpaṇe ||  
  
staranāśanapiṇḍeṣu na grāhyā sapta vai kuśāḥ |  
indhanāni suśuṣkāni yājñiyāniśubhāni ca ||  
  
pāpasaṃbilvapatraṃ ca madhudugdha ghṛtairapi |  
trimarasyāt sāntyarthamabhāve vāyavāstilāḥ ||  
  
pañcāśatāpalaijyeṣṭhai tadarddhairapi madhyame |  
kanyase viṃśati palairargha pātraṃ sa yantrikaṃ ||  
  
homadravyādi pātraṃ nodantādi saṃkhaśuktijaṃ |  
  
130b)  
  
merubhūvṛṣakūrmābjaṃ hematārādi jantathā |  
kūrmapṛṣṭhapṛthvī padmaṃ aṣṭe lohamayaṃ kvacit ||  
  
candanaṃ tilatailādi pātraṃ dīpāḥ sarāvakāḥ |  
hemaṃ kavolikāyugmaṃ raupyaṃ vāhyamadhudvahaṃ ||  
  
phalasaṃpūraṇe deṣa pādābhyaṅga kṛte mataṃ |  
lakṣmyārthammadhuparkārthaṃ śalāke dve suvarṇaje ||  
  
tridvekamāśikete ca jyeṣṭaliṅgādyatu kramāt |  
tathā praśasta sāmagrī śaṣvāṣṭāṃgārghapūritaḥ ||  
  
pātramupatrikāyuktaṃ bhojanārtha sunirvraṇaṃ |  
agnisaṃsthāpane pātramavaṣṭambha dvayānvitaṃ ||  
  
sāvaṣṭambhaṃ sa nālañca ghṛtapātraṃ sukalpitaṃ |  
ghaṇṭāpi susvanādīpa mālāsanye tulādijā ||  
  
ārātrikaṃ sughaṭitaṃ navavartisamanvitaṃ |  
calusthālīdṛcostāmra nirmitāḥ supidhānakāḥ ||  
  
sa tāmra caṭṭakādhūpa dahana sā vṛttinavaḥ |  
gṛhopakare tāmra rūpāni tilakā tathā ||  
  
vṛtsvalpekāṃśya yajñārthe snāpane punaḥ |  
  
131a)  
  
haridrā tailayuktaṃ tadadhvatāmra ghaṭīkratau |  
sakāṃśya khārikādarśau niyugāni vahūnyapi ||  
  
kumbhāghātaraṇe nānā naivedya ṣaṭprakārakaṃ |  
khaṭvā ca bhūlikauśau padhānau śuklauttare cchade ||  
  
netra paṭṭacāmarā khaḍgau cchrarmau pataṃ grahaḥ |  
katvalopaṭṭike padmau candrayugānvitaḥ phaluṃ ||  
  
nānāvastradhṛtāpaṃṭī saṃjñakajalapatrakaṃ |  
madhūkamañjanaṃ kāṇḍapaṭaḥ kāṇḍadhanuḥ pharī ||  
  
maṇḍalārthañca sāmagrī padravalyādi carmajaṃ |  
sa koṣṭajaṃ padmapatraṃ vahujajñopavītakaṃ ||  
  
sindhūraghaṭikātallīkaḍolāpīṭhikāśilāḥ |  
mūśalolūkhale dhanyā mārjanīlavarṇādi ca ||  
  
daṇḍadhavalaṃ cchatraṃ gṛhopakalaṇañca yat |  
yajñiyataṇḍulāraktasūtraṃ caryādi pāduke ||  
  
lohasaṃdaṃśikāvaṃśa nalikāya sapatrikāḥ |  
rocanādi dhṛtau saṃkha pātraṃ hemādi cāśubhaṃ ||  
  
śayyā paṭṭaṃ yogapaṭṭaṃ paṭṭa *? trādi sambhavaṃ |  
  
131b)  
  
pañcāsatāvāṇahanyo syurdaśāntai phalaiḥ kramāt |  
kumbhādyāścānyaliṅgāno kuṃḍakuṇḍe ca varddhinī ||  
  
aṣṭaṣoḍaśaviṃśatyāpyaṅgulai snāna guṃḍikāḥ |  
hīnamadhyottamākṣāpi liṅge hastamite sthire ||  
  
gaḍḍukaiḥ prasthamātra syāt karavṛddhaiṣu cāṣṭabhiḥ |  
vṛddhi phalai bhavenmūrti bhṛtaupiṇḍasaṃkhyayā ||  
  
saṃhitājāpinaḥ śastra jāpinaḥ stotra pāṭhakāḥ |  
tacca devāti nipunāḥ svalpāvāyakṣiṇī mate ||  
  
pratikuṇḍa cārghapātraṃ vyañjanaṃ śrukśruvādi ca |  
śrīparṇī panaśāśokaśākāsvasthādi vṛkṣajā ||  
  
madhyavaktrā vahi pṛṣṭhā mūladaṃṣṭrāśraṣuṣkarāḥ |  
aṣṭayavāditaḥ kāryā ṣaṭviṃśadaṃgulā yathā ||  
  
ekaika dvitri hrāsādvā dveṣārtha bhuja vā kvacit |  
gaurī tantrepi ṣaṭtriṃśāṅgulo śrugvāhu mānavat ||  
  
ādhikyādāyaśuddhyarthaṃ kitvekaṃ maṅgalaṃ kṣipet |  
navāgulaparīnāhā tanmūle dvikalo ghaṭaḥ ||  
  
vṛhadvidyā purāṇepi sa saptāṅgula veṣṭataḥ |  
  
132a)  
  
tanmukhānirgato daṇḍaḥ samonāhāccharāṅgulaḥ |  
ṣaṭvā saptanā kumbhe na tathā gaṇḍikayā saha ||  
  
viṃśatyaṃguladīrghā hi makarādi mukhastvadhaḥ |   
śraiṣṭhe tvekādhiko madhye kanyaśedvyaṅgulādhikaḥ ||  
  
madhyemedvidvivṛddhyā caivaṃ tisraḥ śrucaḥ samāḥ |  
kāmye naimittike nitye śrīnārāyaṇakaṇvataḥ ||  
  
upavedī dvidīrghāsyā pṛṣṭhasyāccaturaṅgulāḥ |  
etasyā madhyato lakṣmī śvārcaṅgī sanmukhī hitāḥ ||  
  
tasyāvahiḥ pārśvayugme dvau siṃhau vikramonnatau |  
aṣṭasaptaraśairvedī jyeṣṭhādyaṅgulamānataḥ ||  
  
sadyañca vedavistīrṇa tanmadhye tryaṅgulaṃ khanet ||  
  
catudvitriḥ palāpūrṇa yathāsaṃmāni tatra tu |  
vartulacaturaśre vā padmāṣṭadalamuṣite ||  
  
ataḥ karṇikayā kiñcinyūnnayā bījayuktayā |  
seśadā śivayā khāte vṛttābdi yavamekhale ||  
  
vedīcitrā samācānte pṛṣṭhe kumbhayutāśadā |  
aṅguṣṭhadvaṇḍayormadhyaṃ saptāṅgulārthato bhavet ||  
  
132b)  
  
vedīvadvistṛtaṃ vaktra māyāmāturagāṅgulaṃ |  
ṣaṭyavaṃ cottamādyeṣu durgā hṛdaya ḍāmare ||  
  
ante tadvistaraṃ tryaṃśādvistṛkaṃ golakena vā |  
mukhāgrakaṇca yorvāsyā vedī tryaṃśena vistaraḥ ||  
  
kaniṣṭhā pṛṣthaniryātaṃ puronisnājya nirgamaḥ |  
lohaśalākayā kārya sthidvarāsyaḥ samaśriye ||  
  
hastoyāmārātmiko vā śruvaḥ śruyyoniruttamaḥ |  
svaśāstravihito cāsyā caturviṃśāṃgulopi vā ||  
  
taṇḍoviṣṭavatsthūlo nādvācaturaṅgulaḥ |  
etadarddhastvadho bhāge madhye sūtrānupātataḥ ||  
  
śrīcaṇḍabhairavasnigdhorgaṇḍī tadagramūlagāḥ |  
kāryākaṅkanavaddaṇḍa syāṇu vṛttañca tryaṅgulaṃ ||  
  
eko mṛgapadākārastatra khātoṃgula dvayaḥ |  
karṣādhārāvaṭosyāntardvipavaḥ seturīśvare ||  
  
kumbhadvaya putapṛṣṭhe daṇḍodvā viṃśadaṅgulaḥ |  
anyo vā tu gugguruḥ sājyaścandanādyarunyapi(?) ||  
  
133a)  
  
muktagranthita puṣpaugo mayoktapuṣpaṃ saṅgrahe |  
karpūraṃ kuṅkumaghṛṣṭa candanañca vilepane ||  
  
tilayavādi homārthaṃ snāne gorocanāmadhuḥ |  
pañcā vā kapilāsthāpyāścatu dvāre samaṇḍape ||  
  
tāsāṃ dugdhādibhiḥ kārya carupākādi vā paraṃ |  
bhaśmagomayaṃ gomutra dadhiśaccharkarādi ca ||  
  
udumbara vaṭāsvaccha *? ptvāmratvaksupīsitaṃ |  
kaśāyañca mṛdaḥ sarvā akeśakarparādikāḥ ||  
  
dvipāvṛṣākṣetramadhyānnadītīra dvayānnagāta |  
śarāsutīrthādvalākā mṛdoṣṭau suska cūrṇitāḥ ||  
  
goṣṭhāścatuspathādrāja dvārādapi varāhataḥ |  
prāguktayuktagovinda mṛtsnā etāśca dvādaśaḥ ||  
  
tīrthābhāsisugandhīni tathārtavaṃ phalāṣṭakaṃ |  
sarvoṣadhi svarṇaratnasasya puṣpaphalāmbu ca ||  
  
śāśṛṅgāṃbhaḥ puṣpaśataṃ sāṣṭaṃ vahuvidhaṃ tathā |  
payodadhighṛtakṣaudra khaṇḍai syāt pañcamādhuryaṃ ||  
  
tilataṇḍulamaṅgaiśca kṛśarāguḍamiśritā |  
ghaṭāsāṣṭaśataṃ snāne pañcavāra ghaṭastathā ||  
  
sahaśraśravadhārau ca kalaśauśatamauṣadhī |  
sahadevāvalāpāṭhā lakṣaṇā ca śatāvarī ||  
  
vijayāti valāvṛddhirguḍavṛddhisuvarcalāḥ |  
snānārtha pṛthagudviṣṭāḥ siddhārthādyāśca rakṣaṇau ||  
  
godhūmayavavilvānāṃ cūrṇanyapi virūkṣaṇe |  
nirmacchanāñca lokokṣa yadvā vajrādi yaiṣṭakaṃ ||  
  
vaiḍūrya vajrapadmapuṣparāgau muktāphalāni ca |  
atinīlanīlasūryakāntāraṣṭāṣṭakaṃnniti ||  
  
uśīraṃ śaṃkhinī kuṣṭaṃ viṣṇukrāntāśatāvarī |  
śrīkhaṇḍamagaruṃ rakta candanaṃ cauṣadhī vrajaḥ ||  
  
śuvarṇarajataṃ kāśyaṃ māraṃsulvasavaṅgakaṃ |  
ayaḥ śīdhakaminyaṣṭau lohānikāṣṭakūṣṭake ||  
  
pārado gandhako vahni gerikābhrakaḍorikāḥ |  
tālaṃ manaḥśilāsvarṇamākṣikandhaṣṭadhātavaḥ ||  
  
yavātilāmāsamuṅgaikaṅgugodhūmasyāmakāḥ |  
  
134a)  
  
nīvārāhrīhayoṣṭatthamanyathā subhago mate |  
aṣṭamuṣṭirbhavet kuṃci kucidaṣṭau tu * *? laṃ ||  
  
catuḥpuṣkala āḍhastaiścaturbhidroṇakādayaḥ |  
iti pañcāṣṭakā prāptau pañcadravyānyu pādadet ||  
  
hāraṃsaṃhāhematālaṃ yavānapi yadā punaḥ |  
sarvābhāvastadāsvarṇaṃ sūtaṃ vā yata karmasu ||  
  
sthāpyā velāvidedvāra valatyāṃ ghaṭikā yathā |  
niṣpattau ṣaṭparāntalpadaṃlāramāguraucchritāḥ ||  
  
tāmrīdvādaśavistīrṇāścaturaṅgulamānayā |  
svarṇamāṣakasūcyāntaḥ kṛtaraṃ pravipajjalaiḥ ||  
  
saṃpūrṇāmati padādaṇḍa ityucyate tadā |  
ahorātraṃ ṣaṣṭidaṇḍaiḥ syādakau dvaudaye dvaye ||  
  
daśakṛṣṇalakomāsataṣṭau śāstraśuvarṇakaḥ |  
śuvarṇo dviguṇakarṣaṃ catuṣkarṣaiḥ palaṃ bhavet ||  
  
snānādhivāsapūjāsu pratiṣṭhāyāñca yugmasaḥ |  
dadyādvāsāṃ śiraṃ pāṇi śilāvedī vṛṣesvapi ||  
  
kuṇḍalairmukuṭaihāre mudrākeyūrakaṃkanaiḥ |  
svarṇopavītairkaṭakaiḥ grāmaratnādi vāhanaiḥ ||  
  
vāśobhipūjayedvitta sādhyahīno guruṃvaraiḥ |  
tatpādapādahīnaiśca mūrtidharādi brāhmaṇān ||  
  
vipravadgatakaṃ mukhyaṃ kāruṃcānyānyathā valaṃ |  
praveśaye snātyajādīna cānyāśramajāṣkṛtau ||  
  
tato mūrtiyavi prādyaiḥ śāntikalādi dvārakān |  
sāntibhūtivalārogya saṃjñātmantoraṇānyaset |  
  
tatsāyoḥ svadakṣādi nandikā pālinau tataḥ |  
bhṛṅgī bhāsyau vṛṣaskandau devī caṇḍau tathottare ||  
  
tryakṣakṛṣya śirānaddhā dhṛṣṭakūrca triśūladhṛk |  
svetakaupīnavānvṛddho bhṛṅgī dṛṣṭokṣabhṛcchikhī ||  
  
vṛṣo vṛṣanibhaḥ śubhraḥ stryakṣassagalakasmalaḥ |  
ghaṇṭhācāmarabhṛtyīno vṛṣāsyo vā pumān kvacit ||  
  
dvivāhu rekāsyā dhvajabhṛddakṣa śakti parorparaṃ |  
tāmracūḍīlohitāṃgaḥ ṣaḍbhujārka karopi vā ||  
  
vibhracchaktyasi vajrāṇi dakṣaghaṇṭhā ca kheṭakaṃ |  
  
135a)  
  
yathākramaṃ sadāṣaṭbhiḥ dakṣiṇottara pāṇibhiḥ |  
ṣaṭtrīṣu pāśanistriṃśa tatadraustarjanī yutaḥ ||  
  
śā * *? ca dakṣiṇe haste ṣaḍbhi vāme kare tathā |  
sikhipicchadhanuḥ kheṭa patākā bhayakukkuṭaiḥ ||  
  
ṣaṭmukhārūpa sampanno yuvāvālotha bhūṣitaḥ |  
hemābhā yuvatī madhya kṣāmapī na ghanastanī ||  
  
viśālanetrā vṛttāsyā'darśayānī bhujā jvalāḥ |  
tatsākhāmūlavinyastau praśāntaśiśirau ghaṭau ||  
  
parjanyāśokasajñā dvau bhūtasaṃjīvanāmṛtau |  
dhanadaśrīpradovasthaṃmaṣṭau pūrvakramādyajet ||  
  
toraṇāsyuryadāpyaṣṭau nyāso dvayo dvayoryathā |  
ṛddhidakīrtidastadvadvṛddhidaḥ puṣṭido paraḥ ||  
  
agnyādī śāntagāḥ pūjyā svadigmaṃtreṇa te kramāt |  
lokagrahe vasuddhāsthaḥ śravastīnāṃ dvayaṃ dvayaṃ ||  
  
bhānu trayaṃ yugavedālakṣmīrgaṇapatistathā |  
yāgaukasindhamīdevāstoraṇestoraṇe sthitāḥ ||  
  
vighnoghadhvaṃsane yajña rakṣapāya ca sādarāḥ |  
  
135b)  
  
vajrādi cakrāntaṃ digpātraṃ patākā svarcayet kramāt |  
vyātī oṃ hū& pha ḥ vajrāya hū& phaṭ ca namastviti ||  
  
ādimantraiṇa śaktyādīnkrāmadagnyādi kīrtanāt |  
kumudaḥ kumudākhyotha puṇḍarīkaśca vāmanaḥ ||  
  
saṅkukarṇasarva netra sumukhaḥ suprasiddhakaḥ |  
supratiṣṭhitaḥ ityarcā sughorā dhvaja devatāḥ ||  
  
oṃ kauṃ kumudāye namaḥ | ityādyairmantrasañcayaiḥ |  
sametābhūtakoṭībhiḥ kṣetrapālāṣṭakaṃ tathā ||  
  
hetukastripuraghnaśca vaṃhnyākhyāyamājihvakaḥ |  
kālakarālī caikāṃghrirbhīmaścāti bhayānakāḥ ||  
  
kaṃṭhyātṛṇoṣve vandheṣu vaṃśe sthūṇāsuvārcayet |  
pṛthyādi pañcatatvāni sadyādyaiḥ pūrvavat tataḥ ||  
  
maṇḍapaṃ śāṅkaraṃ dhāma nivṛttyādi kalāmayaṃ |  
sādāśivaṃ tatvaṃ garbhaṃ patākāśakti lakṣitaṃ ||  
  
paśyaṃtatva dṛśā prāgva praviśyātmādiśodhanaṃ |  
kṛtvā svātmādimabhyarcya lalāṭakaṇṭha pādagān tatvatatveśvarāt mūrti   
mūrtīśākhānubhi nyaset |  
  
136a)  
  
ete karaṇa bhūtātma śivamantrāḥ śiva pradāḥ |  
idaṃ ca mūrti mūrtīśa tatvatrayaṃ śarīrakaṃ ||  
  
liṅgabrahma śilāpīṭhaṃ śodhya bodhyatvamāgata |  
ityādyālocya saṃpūjya dikyāndharmādikāntathā ||  
  
vedyadhodikṣanaṃntādīn prāgvaghāṭāluke tataḥ |  
maṇḍale sthaṇḍile kumbha vahnau vā śivamarcayet ||  
  
svamantramūrtipātyasya saṃhitā jāpinastathā |  
asaṃkhyātāstramantraika parānapyastra jāpinaḥ ||  
  
vidikṣudīkṣitāndakṣānstato viprānpaṭhanti ca |  
vṛṣākapiṃ yāvamāṇīṃ śrīsuktañca samaitrakaṃ ||  
  
japedṛgvedaviprocit saumyāyāṃ vāpi dakṣiṇe |  
stambasūktātharvaṃ śiro nīlarudronatharvacit ||  
  
ślokādhyāya yajupratyagrudrañca mūktabrāhmaṇyai |  
sāmavedyantare deva vrataṃ sāmacārathantaraṃ jyeṣṭha somasāmāniyā vasānikā |  
  
puruṣagatiñca vṛtaḥ suratānekaroditnit(?) |  
ṛgvedī yadi vā pūrve sāmavedī tu dakṣiṇe ||  
  
yajurvedī paścimayāmatharvottarato japet |  
ta āhitādaro yāvakuṇḍegni janayedguruḥ ||  
  
tāvantadājñayā kuṇḍalābhimagne nidhāya ca |  
astra japta yutā mūrtiḥ dharā kupyu viśodhanaṃ ||  
  
bhūtānāmarghapātrañca kuśatakuptaśāntrikumbhaṃ saṃpātyoktaṃ   
dhruvāsanaṃ |  
guruścainaṃ kṛtvāthāgni nisvāsaśekhare yathā ||  
  
iśādyajāntai nitye syān naimitīke nyathā tataḥ |  
īśatat puruṣājātā vāmāghoraiśca kāmyake ||  
  
īśāghorasadyo vāma purumāntai mukhaikatā |  
sasvasvabījairurddha prā sva gdakṣontarerapi ||  
  
snānaṃ sandhyā tathā pūjā japo homa ca pañcamaḥ |  
iti nityāṅgamubdiṣvaṃ pavitraṃ damanantathā ||  
  
dīkṣā caiva pratiṣṭhā ca naimittikamidaṃ dvayaṃ |  
animādi prasiddhiśca kāmyantadapi vistaraṃ ||  
  
granthyanādi pallavāntaṃ nisāsaṃcāra iritaṃ |  
  
137a)  
  
mantrasādhyākṣaraikaikaṃ granthanaṃ brahmayāmale |  
dvābhyāmantrākṣaraikacaiḥ sādhyamekaṃ vidarbhanaṃ ||  
  
vāmadakṣiṇato mantraṃ sādhyorodhaṃ himālaye |  
caturdikṣu padāmantraṃ saṃpuṭaṃ kāmike tadā ||  
  
mantrayogāgrataḥ sādhyaṃ pallavaṃ tadviparyayāt |  
svāhā śāntau svadhā puṭau vauṣaddaśyenamārcane ||  
  
ṭha ṭha stambhe phaṭ | cāryamāraṇo ghāṭaya dvayaṃ |  
vaṣaḍākarṣane jāti eṣākṣāpyanyathohitāḥ ||  
  
granthane śāntike proktaṃ vasyākṛṣṭāvidarbhane |  
stobhamānaṃ maṭaṃrodhe sampuṭe stambha kīlanaṃ ||  
  
vidveśoccāṭanaṃ yoge pallave māraṇaṃ kuruḥ |  
hemavante poṣṭikaṃ karma śiśire māraṇaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
vaśyā kṛṣṇe vasantepi grīṣme vidveṣanaṃ mahat |  
prāvṛṣyapi mahoccāṭaṃ śāntaṃ śaradiśaṃ śraye ||  
  
tathā yoge ca hemantaṃ prabhāte śiśiraṃ viduḥ |  
prahareṇa vaśantañca madhyāhne grīṣmamanthnāṃḥ ||  
  
praharatraye varṣāstu śaradamamastameṣu ca |  
  
137b)  
  
atha kṛtvā kuṇḍasaṃkhyān bhāgānpūrvādiśāṅguruḥ |  
prāgādi kuṇḍeṣvāropyate pīśāvāhanādikaṃ ||  
  
kṛtvā dhyātvā pratapyanti śivaṃ svānu svarūpiṇaṃ |  
deśikaścāpi vidhinā vahnināsautvanantakaṃ ||  
  
nālahṛdavadhidhyātvā tasthapadmercayecchivaṃ |  
jvālājihvānu sāreṇa prāgādīśānta madhyataḥ ||  
  
rakṣodādāhe jananī mṛtyudā satruhārikā |  
vaśaṃkarī mahoccāṭā dhanadāmukti sādhikāḥ ||  
  
sarvakāmapradā madhye tasmāt madhye tu homayet |  
dadyāt pūrṇa dvayaṃ jihvā kliṣṭāsaṃnidhi śivena tu ||  
  
lavarṇādayakṣāntā vahni ṣaṣṭhasurāśrayāḥ |  
sārddhacandrabinduśikhā jihva bījāni vedikaiḥ ||  
  
narādyairka vacādyaiśca pūrvādoyaṃ ca kuṇḍake |  
madhyendhī śaśivānubhyaṃ navādiṣvapi homayet ||  
  
navaṣvindrādau vahnyādau narādyaiśca dayādibhiḥ |  
ṣoḍaśādiṣu vaktrā'ṅgaiḥ sarvāturvaika kuṇḍakaṃ ||  
  
138a)  
  
vāstvādi homaṃ nirvartya vali prāgvaccaruṃ tathā |  
nivedya pratikuṇḍañca nāndīśrādhavidhāyinā ||  
  
guruśca kṛtanāndīka kartādau prāgvadvārcitaḥ |  
koṣadhvajavitālākhya snānaṃ sadmetra vaiditaḥ ||  
  
tatrāśanainyaśelliṅgaṃ dhruvenāstreṇa varmanā |  
tāḍanāllekhane kṛtvā kṛtvā bhyarcya bhuvena tu ||  
  
careyākarasuddhyarthaṃ hu phaḍantāśināsphuṭaṃ |  
samūrtiyo mala snānaṃ liṅgādīnā dvidāgame ||  
  
mṛtasnākayāyagomūtraśāsakṛdbhaśmakaṇṭhakaiḥ |  
iṣṭvā carmavāśasthanaṃ svetapuṣpaistatorcayet ||  
  
sāmānyānunā tu prāgvat pratyagvedyādhruvāśane |  
śayyāyāṃ nyasyaśallakṣa bhakteghna sṛṇatantunā ||  
  
somyāsyāmaṅgalailiṅge guruḥ salākayo kṣiret |  
tadeva samarkālaṃ tu śilpī'śastreṇa vartrayet ||  
  
mānonmānapramānādi vikalpepyuditaṃ yadi |  
lakṣmyāstistatra sānidhyamavaśyaṃ pātidevatāḥ ||  
  
138b)  
  
arcāddhyāstryaṃ śataḥ pādā śubhaṃ lakṣmyā vatāraṇaṃ |  
yavaṃ tu navadhā kṛtvā'ṣṭāgairekhā tu hāstike ||  
  
arcāṅgula pramānaiśca yavaiścaiva yavāṃśakaiḥ |  
lakṣmyadeho praviṣṭāro rekhānisnā ca vistṛtāḥ ||  
  
dviyavaddhyaṃsavṛddhiḥ syāt sāntereṣu yathākramaṃ |  
lakṣmadehe ca rekhāyāṃ tryaśātyakṣāvatāraṇaṃ ||  
  
aṣṭabhaktasame tasmi pṛṣṭhe yogo dvivarjanāt |  
tatra ca saṅgamaḥ kāryaḥ pakṣayo nāgapāśavat ||  
  
tribhakte'rddhaparityāgādvramo vā sarvakāmadaḥ |  
tai tadvāma cale lobhe īśāne calarohayoḥ ||  
  
svākāro lakṣaṇaṃ teṣāṃ ratneṣu teja ujvalaṃ |  
tārātryaṃśato netronmīlanaṃ pratimāsvapi ||  
  
tatryaṃśākyātirityetallakṣaṇannataradvitaṃ |  
tāṃ rekhāṃ madhu sarpisyāṃ mṛtyuṃjitā prapūrya ca ||  
  
śilpidoṣanivṛtyarthaṃ snapaye tatmṛdādibhiḥ |  
saṃdhūpyeṣṭvārcayet kāruṃ sapyāpātra śalākayā ||  
  
139a)  
  
sthāpakāya tato deyāḥ śaktiścet pañcadhenavaḥ |  
liṅgamiṣṭvā japettailairdūrvākāṇḍa śatena ca ||  
  
sa bhartṛputrānāryā'ṣṭau gāyantyaḥ śuddhavaṃśajāḥ |  
savyopasavyasūtreṇa spṛśe yutāḥ kuśena vā ||  
  
saṃsnāpya rocanāṃ datvā kuryu nirmatsanaṃ yatāḥ |  
dadyātāsāṃ dhanyākaparyaṭaṃ lavanaṃ guḍaṃ ||  
  
siṃdūraṃ sūtikāṃ dhūcāmalaktaṃ kajjalāti ca |  
hṛdādhruvena vā paścāt mūrti bhṛtsaṃhito guruḥ ||  
  
sṛṅgosakṛtmūtra sakṛtmūrti bhaśmadugdhai prāgvantu saṃskṛtaiḥ |  
paṃcagavyā mṛtaiḥ pañca valkalairoṣadhī jalaiḥ ||  
  
rudrai hṛdā vā guhyeṇa snāpayet pañcamādhuraiḥ |  
śatapuṣpāṃvubhiḥ nānā phalāṣṭaka jalena ca ||  
  
yavagodhūmavilvānāṃ cūrṇaivudvartryaganvibhiḥ |  
svacchairgandhayutāṣṭaubhiḥ sarvoṣadhyaṣubhistataḥ ||  
  
ratnakāñcana gośṛṅgaḥ dhānyagaṅgādi vāribhiḥ |  
sahaśradhārādighaṭai sa candana jalena ca ||  
  
139b)  
  
vidyeśvarāṣṭakumbhaiśca śivakumbena śaktitaḥ |  
svetavastreṇa sanmārjya pādyaṃ saṃrodhasaṃnidhī ||  
  
kṛtvā sadyena sampūjya brahmabhiḥ sakalī caraṇa |  
āvāhyā lipye vājyena gandhadravyendu candanaiḥ carmaṇā vā śaśīrakto   
paridhāṣyotha bhūṣayet |  
  
īśenamālyaprakaraiḥ siddhārtha tilakāṅkitaṃ |  
vahurūpena nīrājya puṃṣāṣṭāṅgena cārghayet ||  
  
iśenā cāmyasarvātma deve neṣṭvā japaṃ stutiṃ |  
vidhāyaliṅgamutthāpya hṛdā bhavāṃ budviṣṇavāṃ ||  
  
suyaṃtrite rathe nyasya saṃkhādyāḍamvaraiḥ puraṃ |  
prāsāda bhrāmayedyaddhā yatnato'tha purakṣipan ||  
  
kāṃśyavāsau hiraṃnyādīnsapta vrīhīnsa puṣpakān |  
deśikaḥ prokṣite deśe yajvārathāgrato vrajet ||  
  
pade pade svamedhānāṃ koṭī vā phalamāpnuyāt |  
pañcāpātakino ye ca te yānti paramāṅgatiṃ ||  
  
140a)  
  
pradakṣiṇaṃ paribhrāmya yāgauko dvāri paścime |  
pūrvāsyaṃ bhadrapīṭhasthaṃ hṛdāsaṃpūjya cārghayet ||  
  
kṛte svastyapane saṃmya praveśa hṛdayena tu |  
vedī madhye nyaset paṭṭaṃ sudāruṃ kauśikogrataḥ ||  
  
khaṭvāṃ vā śikhayā kṛṣṭa gaṃḍuvarmāmvarā vṛtaṃ |  
anantena dhruvenātha tūlikāmāstaraistataḥ ||  
  
pūrvoktamāsanaṃ tatra datvotthāpya hṛdā prabhuṃ |  
prasvāpyaśirasā pūrva mūrdhnānamathavā śati ||  
  
vedyāṃśata maṇḍale tasyāḥ pratīcyāntaṃ tato hṛda |  
samarpyābhyarcya tāreṇa deveśāne ghaṭa nyaset ||  
  
nidrākhyaśatakṛtvastra japtaṃ ghoreṇa vāśinā |  
punarliptvā hṛdāliṅgaṃ saṃdhūpyācchādya vāśasā ||  
  
kavace nātha naivedyaṃ datvā nānā prakāravat |  
gṛhopakaraṇaṃ khaḍga pataṅgrahādi vādhunā ||  
  
abhyaṅga ye pādadeśe madhvājya pātramaurcavit |  
hṛdoṅgīthena vā ghore nāthaliṅgāntare varāṃ ||  
  
liṅgavat pūjitāṃsnātāṃ kriyākhyāṃ pīṭhavigrahāṃ |  
liptāṃ vastrāvṛtāṃ kliptaraṃdhrastha bhagalakṣaṇāṃ ||  
  
prāgukta āsananyasya śirasā pūjayedvṛdā |  
prācyāmadhyāṃ nyaselliṅgaṃ dhāsripratyagmukhe sadā ||  
  
piṇḍī brahmaśilādyañca pratīcyāmathaprāgmukhe |  
kāryaviparyayāt sarvaṃ tato brahmaśilāmapi ||  
  
pañcaratnādi sampanā liṅge mūlercitāṃ nyaset |  
vṛṣañca saṃskṛtaṃ sviṣṭaṃ piṇḍikottarato hṛdā ||  
  
dhruvena vārpayedevaṃ catvāryāpādyayuktitaḥ |  
kuśabhaśmatilaivāhya ghorāstra kavacaiścaret ||  
  
dikṣupuṣpanyasta puṣpaśarāṃ dadyāntri bhāga buddhaye ||  
  
hṛdaivānupādadeśe guraḥ sthitvānyaśennayān |  
ā& ī& ū& mantrabhistatva trayaṃ dīkṣokta vyāptikaṃ ||  
  
sādhipaṃ caturaśrāśra vṛtteṣu keśanāmasu |  
pratibhāgaṃ krame naiva sṛṣṭā pūrvāditastataḥ ||  
  
pṛthivyagnyātma sūryāṃstu vāyu candra nabhāṃ śiva |  
vinyaset mūrtirūpāṇi mantrā caiṣāṃ narādayaḥ ||  
  
mūrtiśāḥ sarva paśupatyugrarudrabhavāṃstataḥ |  
īśānaśca mahādevo bhīmaśca kṛtaḥ puraḥsarāḥ ||  
  
vidyeśāna śuddhabhogārthaṃmaśuddhyarthañca lokayān |  
bhairavānkṣudraśidhyartha mūrtipatvena yojayet ||  
  
dhārikā dīptimatyugrā jyotsnā cetāvalotkaṭā |  
dhātrī vitvī cayoṣārthāsthāpana mūrtināyakāḥ ||  
  
kṣamādyā mūrtayatvaṣṭau dhārikādyāṣṭakethavā |  
vāmādayotha mūrtīsya paṃcakuṇḍepi mūrtayaḥ ||  
  
kṣāṃvutejomaruṅgāni keśeśāna śadāśivāḥ |  
mūrtīśā bhuktaye muktyai nivṛtyādi kalākilaḥ ||  
  
sadyodi devatāścātha stryarcā mūrtidharādikāḥ |  
vāmādyeṣu kriyāṃ cānya icchāveti tadīśvarāḥ ||  
  
vinārai caitā mūrtayo sthitāḥ | ugrārddhānāntamāmohā ghorāratirapajvarāḥ |   
mūrtiṇā mūrtayaḥ sadyo ityaṣṭau pañcadhānyaset ||  
  
141b)  
  
tamodi mūrtigāvārtha droveśāntaka mohakṛt |  
rati nāyaka dīkṣiruddhā mūrtīso bindu gahvare ||  
  
liṅgādi sthāpakā liṅga dehāraṃbhaika hetavaḥ |  
tataḥ śaraccandra kānti sarvātmabhirabhedinaṃ ||  
  
gururdvyāpedviśeṣena liṅgātmānaṃ punaḥ śivaṃ |  
aṣṭatriṃśatkalanyasya tasyādhiṣṭhāyakaṃ tathā ||  
  
sāṅganityavadīśena muktakuṇḍalādi ca |  
puruṣenāñjanaṃ svarghaṃ rocanādarpaṇantathā ||  
  
rūpiṇā kaṭisūtrañca brahmasūtrā gadādikaṃ |  
vitānaṃ cāmaracchatraṃ dhvajādi guhyakena ca ||  
  
lehya cosya haviṣyādi sadyena hṛdayena vā |  
itthaṃ pīṭhabrahmaśilā vṛṣabheṣu śilādikāḥ ||  
  
mūrtyādi vinyasedyogī kriyāśakti padetatu |  
oṃkārādyena oṃ sū& hū& vījānyatarayogināḥ ||  
  
natyante nātha oṃ hrī& śamahāgaurī padāntaraṃ |  
rudradayite svāheti mantreṇā vāhya pūjayet ||  
  
142a)  
  
mandarerāvatpiṇḍakriyāśaktyandikṣāntataḥ |  
dhyātvā brahmaśilāṃ visvādhāramūrtyādi kalpitāṃ ||  
  
vartanīṃ samavāyenau hrī& jñānaśaktaye namaḥ |  
itīṣṭvā sannidhāyai nāmanasā bhāvayet sphuṭaṃ ||  
  
oṃ hā& dharmāya namaḥ | ityantena hṛdaye nama | samāvā *?   
kriyāśaktiṃ vyāpinaṃ vṛṣamarcayet | kuṇḍamadhye pareśāna mekhalāmupe   
  
nābhauśevīkiyā śaktiṃ nādaṃ coṣṭavicintayet |  
vahnisthena ghaṭasthena mūrtipaiśca parasparaṃ ||  
  
nāḍīsaṃdhānakaṃ kuryāt prāgvasnīlapatāpatākacit |  
mūrtimūrtiśvarāṃ kuṇḍai svāvāhya mūrtiyānapi ||  
  
svarūpamūrtisāmarthya vyāptiḥ saṃdhāna yoginaḥ |  
pūrṇācchinnatarpayet | brahmāṅge brāhmaṅgeśca yathākramaṃ ||  
  
tatastu saṃnidhau teṣāṃ saṃhitā homamīpsayā |  
kṛtvā brahmāṅgakaṃ spṛṣṭvā śāntikumbhombhasā kuśaiḥ ||  
  
svāṅgadaśa * *?mūnthapeyu homasaṃkhyayā |  
  
142b)  
  
ācāryaḥ sarvasandhāna yogakṛnnavadhā sthitaḥ |  
yogivanmūrti mūrtīśānā vāhya svānunā tataḥ ||  
  
mūlenāṅgaiśca juhuyāt pṛṣṭvā śānti ghaṭāmbunā |  
prāgvajjapedbrahma bhāgaśuddhau gurvādayastataḥ ||  
  
lū& lū& rū& rū& sū& sū& ṣū ṣū vū& vū& yū& yū& kū& kū& |   
ityauṃkārādi yugmaistu kṣityādyainamasā yutaiḥ |  
śuddhāvi'suddhayoḥ sandhikurpyu vāhmaddhruvādibhiḥ |  
brahmācyutāṃśayoḥ sarga rakṣādharmavatoḥ sadā ||  
  
kṛṣṇalohitayormāyā sadeśa tatva vyāpinau |  
hṛdaiva saṃnedhiṃ kuryu varmanārodhaguṇṭhane ||  
  
itthaṃ saṃdhitaṃ viṣṇuśāḥ sandadhīranharena ca |  
saṃhāravarmaṇātyanta svetana kramaso bhṛṣaṃ ||  
  
kuṇḍalasya vaśānastha svarūpena kramāt tataḥ |  
śivatatvañca sa śuddhaṃ pareṇa'didhīt ||  
  
nyūnānyathā vidhaumūlaṃ svaśuddhau ca śata hunet |  
tvatsakti preritai karma bhagasvaṃstvadanujñayā ||  
  
143a)  
  
nivartitamihāsmābhi bhūyonyantartumādiśaḥ |  
oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya rudraraudra namostute ||  
  
vidhipūrṇamapūrṇaṃ vā śaktyāpūrva pragṛhyatāṃ |  
oṃ hrī& śāṅkari pūraya pūraya svāheti piṇḍyā ||  
  
śrotrai nivedayeyuśca liṅge jñānītatorcaset |  
kriyāpīṭhe tathā dhāra śaktiṃ brahmaśilopari ||  
  
saṃnirodhādi kurvīta vistaroyamathālpake |  
ādhāraśaktimāropyābhyarcya datvāhuti trayaṃ ||  
  
tritatvaṃ pūrvavadvyāpi svasvākāra'dhiyānvitaṃ |  
saṃsāratatparijñānaṃ mukti sāmarthyasaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
svamantrervātha mūlena saṃpūjya tarpayet tataḥ |  
liṅge nyasejjñāna cakṣu liṅge dehakaraparaṃ ||  
  
āvāhya kuṇḍe cābhyarcya hutvā śodhya jayadrathe |  
vidadhīta japaṃ liṅge prāgvatgovindase kecit ||  
  
dvayoḥ sandhiñca kurvati nyāsañca keśīlādikeḥ |  
liṅge dīkṣāviśuddhārtha kāryā kalpanayoditāḥ ||  
  
143b)  
  
dīkṣaye jatānantu nāsau māheśvarau yadi |  
kuryādekatripañcādi divaśānadhivāsanaṃ ||  
  
sadyo vā pratyahaṃ homa śataṃ svasvānubhirbhajet |  
agnisthalādītsaṃrudhya prāgvadbhūtavalindatat ||  
  
rātrau jāgarakṛdvyāyana liṅgādi prakriyāṃ svapet |  
  
adhivāsaḥ ||  
  
atha pūrvavadanyadyurdvisthāniṣṭhā samurtipaḥ |  
śivātsārghaparaḥ śambhu kuṇḍaliṅgaṃ sa pīṭhakaṃ ||  
  
kaśiletdrādikātasvaṣṭasthā prāgvatsamarpayet |  
tarpitāgni śivastacca vijñāpito svarau vrajet ||  
  
kṛtātrayañjarodhāmatatmadhye vedhadoṣahṛt |  
padāsyādeka sūtrantu vedyededhaka madhyagaṃ ||  
  
vādhājñeyastadetyuktaṃ viccandrahāsayoḥ |  
tayormadhena madhyasya pañcanaṃ śreyaśai bhavet ||  
  
avañcanamanarthāya śrīvāyurādi mūditāṃ |  
dvāḥ ṣaṭtriṃśacchatāṃśena brahmasthānaṃ vinirṇayam ḥ ||  
  
tilena vā tilārddhena kiñcidīśānamāśritāṃ |  
jñānaivamādyaṃ śaktyastu kūrmākhyaṃ pūrvanirmitāḥ ||  
  
rasakūrmānvitāṃ nyasya brahmaśilocimevaṭāṃ |  
śaktyanta na śive nātha pūrvoktakaśilānunā ||  
  
oṃ namo vyāpini sthire'caledhrave tataḥ paṭhet |  
laṃ hrī& svāheti cā nandasaṃjñāmāganadhāriṇīṃ ||  
  
sthirāṃ śivasya sañcintya sṛṣṭyā brahmaśilā nyaśet |  
tasyā samastamadhvānaṃ māruḍhaṃ bhāvayed guruḥ ||  
  
tvameva paramāśakti tvamevāsanadhāriṇi |  
śivājñayā tvayā devi sthātadhyamiha sarvadā ||  
  
tāgandhadigvāmabhyarcya sarundhrendrādi dikṣupi |  
ratnoṣadhīlohadhātu bījonto kramān nyaśet ||  
  
dīptyārogya dehavīrya tṛptiśakti mayāni tu |  
loke ca vā cakrairmantrai sarva vā sarvagattake ||  
  
pūrvoktamapyasaṃbhūtau paścāt padmena saṃyutaṃ |  
svarṇavāṃ kṛṣarāṃ sūrisampade śrī vivṛddhaye ||  
  
ghataṃ gorocanāṃ dūrvā hemaśāśṛṅgamṛrtikāṃ |  
  
144b)  
  
godhūmaṃkaśilā svabhre vṛṣañca dvārasaṃmukhaṃ |  
samanna *?lkanaṃ nyaśeccāturvarṇebhi nandane ||  
  
catuspadānā vṛddhyarthaṃ sadā casarpye sampade |  
śrīkāmo deśa vṛddhyai vā madhūkakṣatamañjanaṃ ||  
  
sameruñca nyaset tatra tataḥ prajā samṛddhaye |  
pṛthyā saharpayet sarvaṃ bījānihātakantathā ||  
  
kattasukhodayerāṣṭra vṛddhyainiryagrajāmṛdaṃ |  
mahānadī tīre yugmau cchādārūpyaṃ yavānapi ||  
  
kūrmeṇāropayedyuktā teṣāmānaśca kathyate |  
padmādi hāstike māso navamo sonadāntike ||  
  
hāstikepyoṣadhādīni guṃjānāmnāni pūrvavat |  
ityekatamameveṣāṃ madhyagarbha niveśayet ||  
  
ratnādibhi mahānantaḥ mantranā hṛdayena vā |  
sanatkumāraśāndre tu nyāsopyeṣāṃ kramāt tataḥ ||  
  
iti brahmaśilā nyāsaṃ samāpya vidhinā tataḥ |  
lepayenniva arthaṃ tatpāyasena pureṇa vā ||  
  
varmanā netravastreṇa cchādayitvā valikiret |  
  
145a)  
  
śilāsūtracchidraṃ cchidraṃ śāntyai bhakṣeṇa vāśinā |  
hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ devānvāstu deha gatānapi ||  
  
prāgvatsaṃtarpya pūrṇānte rātrau vāhni subhakṣaṇe |  
dūrvākṣatārcitaṃ liṅgaṃ prāgvadutthāpya cālayet ||  
  
gurustadagra tato gacchamūrtiyā svasvadikṣvapi |  
yajvāpi sasuhṛtpṛṣṭe liṅgaspṛśannathotsavaiḥ ||  
  
devamātrānye prāsāda dvārasamukhaṃ mānayet |  
suviśrāntakṣaṇaṃ tatra dvāraṃ vatvaṃ vinā śivaṃ ||  
  
veśayedvārodveśena yadvā dvāre śikhojjhite |  
dvāro'rddhena praveśa syāt sarvatra śaśikhe punaḥ ||  
  
saspṛśadvāramadhyena nayet tatra sthitaṃ prabhu |  
bhadrapīṭhe dvāravaktamuktāsthiro bhaveditaṃ ||  
  
aśināsodhayecchubhramapanīya paṭaṃ tataḥ |  
saṃpūrṇamāsanaṃ nyasya mukṣayeccandanādibhiḥ ||  
  
yantreṇa dhārayelliṅgaṃ lambanaiḥ praguṇī kṛtaṃ |  
samūrtiko guruśśakti tadvatorvarmadharmiṇoḥ ||  
  
145b)  
  
abhedañcintayet mūlaṃ layānta prāgvandraccaran |  
liṅgati veśayet sṛṣṭyā sa deśābha * *? dhyataḥ ||  
  
digvidigyaujitairaṣṭa śīsakavibhirāyataiḥ |  
pūrṇasikatayā kṛtvā svabhraṃ pīṭhādikaṃ nyaset ||  
  
vyāpakañca paratatvaṃ nyaselliṅge yathāpurā |  
sphuṭe kaṃpite bhrānte śīrṇe vakrena te kvacit ||  
  
sa * *? dāra pūjyādi doṣāyasyādbhavaṃ tṛtaḥ |  
mūlena rūpiṇāvātha satasamudratiddhunet ||  
  
liṅgasaṃsthādhyamānaṃ syādvirodyasyānantaṃ nisi |  
tadvigīśānunā hutvā śataṃ dhāmnā ca śuddhyati ||  
  
vijñāpyātha sataṃ mūlaṃ pūrṇantaṃ pūrvavaddhunet |  
uktānukte doṣajāte śaivī vā śāntiriṣyate ||  
  
mūrti brahmāṇi tatvāni tatve śāśca yajecchivaṃ |  
varmāstrarodhite liṅge tatparaspara lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
sveta vāsā yugacchannāṃ kriyākhāṃ śaktinaiścarī |  
pīṭhabandhavināyomā mantreṇodvo piṇḍikāṃ ||  
  
prāgvadānīyaśahūntaṃ pūrvamantraṃ vicintayet |  
  
146a)  
  
kṛtvottara praṇālaṃ tu vinyaset sṛṣṭimārgataḥ |  
gatārka candrasaṃsarge kalāmṛtā yathaikatāṃ ||  
  
tadvadṛkkriye yoścāpiścaraṇḍaṃ bhāvaye sphuṭaṃ |  
na cetsā praguṇā tasyāścālane rūpinā śataṃ ||  
  
dviguṇaṃ vātha mūlena hunet kailāśa bhāṣanāt |  
lohamalakṣīraśastha cūrṇasarjavipācitaiḥ ||  
  
tailai vālukayā garbha randhraṃ sampūrya snāpayet |  
śāṃtyadbhiḥ pañca madhuraiḥ śāntarai gandha vāribhiḥ ||  
  
piṇḍāmāliṅgamīśaste prāgvallikhyayā spṛśet |  
śivāśanaṃ mantrai tatvānāṃśeśvaraṃ trayaṃ ||  
  
nyasya mūrti nyaselliṅge dhyātvā vidyātmarūpiṇīṃ |  
paraṃ tatvaṃ tadaṅgāni jñānaśaktiśivātmake ||  
  
pīṭhe kriyāṃ samāvāhya saṃsthāpya pūjayet tataḥ |  
vibhūṣya devaṃ vastrādyaiḥ sa ghṛtaṃ guguluṃ dahet ||  
  
vyāpi tvaina śivaṃ dikṣu nyasyāgāni ca nityavat |  
eva sarvatra sānidhyaṃ jīvanyāsena kārayet ||  
  
krīḍā nṛtyādyakasmādya taccihnaṃ sannidhe dhruvaṃ |  
  
146b)  
  
naivedya japa tatpādau vijñāpyeti kṣamāpayet |  
yāvaccandraśca sūryaśca yāvatiṣṭhati medinī ||  
  
mantrai *? lokapālaiśca sthātavyaṃ svacchayā vibhoḥ |  
liṅgasya piṇḍikāghāṭā cchiro jaṭharaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ ||  
  
vraṇe kramād bhavet mṛtyu bhikṣaṃrāṣṭravibhramaḥ |  
tasya śāntirbhaved rūpi śataicāṣṭādhike hute ||  
  
vijñāpite śive paścāt svānuhatpraṇavaistu vā |  
agnai nyasya vṛṣa ceṣṭvā prabhūtapradadedvaliṃ ||  
  
śatanyunānyathā bhāve śataṃ mṛtyuñjayena ca |  
śivena samidhāṃ homaṃ śāntyartha pāyasena ca ||  
  
hṛdā ghoreṇa vārudhya bhavaṃ vijñāpayet punaḥ |  
jñānato jñānato vāya cchāstroktaṃ na kṛtaṃ mayā ||  
  
tatsarvaṃ pūrṇamevāstu tvat prasādāt maheśvaraḥ |  
athāmukeśvarāyeti saṃmyagvṛttimpradāpayet ||  
  
dinatuṣṭayaṃ kuryā sānnadānaṃ mahotsavaṃ |  
śataṃ śatañca kuṇḍeṣu dvitīyahanimūrtipāḥ ||  
  
homaṃ kuryuraghoreṇa prāyaścittāya munnaye |  
tṛtīya divase śāntyai ghṛtākta samidhāṃ śataṃ ||  
  
147b)  
  
dvayaṃ vā pratikuṇḍaṃ tu caturthe prathamethavā |  
dvaye traye vā kurvīta caturthī karmaśeṣakataḥ ||  
  
vāgīśyā brahmabhiḥ svāṅgaiścaruṅkṛtvā yathoditaṃ |  
saṃpātaśuddhakuṇḍeṣu sahaśra vahurūpiṇā ||  
  
yadvā śivenāṅgavatā hutvā devāyataṃ dadet |  
ityuktaṃ liṅgakalpādau caturthī karmanirmalaṃ ||  
  
devānāmapiścānyeṣāṃ(?) svapatnī samvarādibhiḥ |  
athāto devamabhyacya dhūpayitvā hṛdāparaṃ ||  
  
vihāyaliṅgacaitanyaṃ svānumātraṃ visarjayet |  
praṇaveṇāsanādīni nyasyate naiva pūjayet ||  
  
visargaḥ śaktibhāvosmin vyaktirāvāhanādikaṃ |  
paścād kumbha dvayaṃ ceṣṭyā śivakumbhoktanītivat ||  
  
nirmālyādhanayatveka kumbhena snāpayed vibhuṃ |  
dugdhādibhiśca saṃsnāpya yajet pūrvavadīśvaraṃ ||  
  
nipatyavijñāpyamuhuṃ prāgvaccaṇḍa ca pūjayet |  
caṇḍeśvara prapanno yena te *? bhayakāraṇaṃ ||  
  
tasmādārādhanākṣīṇā śaivaṃ panthānamāśritāḥ |  
yena viplutimāpannaṃ brahmādi * *? śaktikaṃ ||  
  
caṇḍarūpaḥ svayaṃ śambhurniruṇadvyāpi niṣkṛtaṃ |  
snānahomajapādyene pratiṣṭhāya vidhānataḥ ||  
  
mūrtivaktrāṅgasaṃyuktamādhāraḥ śakti paṅkaje |  
svasthāne prāṇamārgeṇa kṛtvātmasthaṃ niveśayet ||  
  
aiśānyā jagatī vāhye prāsādagarbhasammite |  
khahrame nyasya taṃ brūyā samaye daṇḍanāyakaṃ ||  
  
tiṣṭanādhvasadārakṣan śivadravyaṃ śivāntike |  
vastrārtha bhūṣaṇaṃ hitvā nirmālyaṃ vartanaṃ cava ||  
  
śivavacantaṃ samabhyarcya bhaktyāvijñāpayediti |  
yanyūnādi kṛtaṃ jñānādajñādvāmayā prabho ||  
  
pūrṇamastveva tatsarvaṃ tṛpto bhava kṣamasvame |  
yāvalliṅgesti devāyaṃ tāvat stheyaṃ tvayāntike ||  
  
sthirārcāyāñca suvyakte sahaśraśatasajñake |  
avyakte mukhyaliṅge ca praśastā caṇḍakalpanāḥ ||  
  
caṇḍaṃ svayaṃ bhūgarbhāsthaṃ vāṇaliṅge tu piṇḍike |  
  
148a)  
  
ghaṭite tu jagatyā vai calai caṇḍo na vidyate |  
svayaṃbhuve vāṇaliṅge mahadbhirya pratiṣṭhitaṃ ||  
  
advetamantra yukte ca na caṇḍo'dhi kṛto bhavet |  
śastraśāṣṭaśataṃ japtvā mano vāktantrabhiḥ śivaṃ ||  
  
natvā datvādikṣu valiṃ bhūvā nirodhayet tataḥ |  
yāvat saṃnihito devo vidyeśvarairiha ||  
  
yāvat saṃnihito bhūto bhūtāyūyaṃ tiṣṭhata bhāvitāḥ |  
pratiṣṭhānte kvacit proktaṃ sthirādyāhuti saptakaṃ ||  
  
sthiro hya prameyo nādi vādho nityotha sarvagaḥ |  
avināśī ca tṛptaśca sthirādyā saptate guṇāḥ ||  
  
paripūraṇāya ca vidhi tṛptaye vahumūrtaye |  
śivāyāhutayo devāḥ sannidhau kvacin matāḥ ||  
  
tataḥ sa bandhayajñānaṃ snāpayet prāgyaṭāmbhasā |  
mūrtyāmekaṃ guruṃ padme sthalavā'lpehni vā tadāḥ ||  
  
abhyarcya śivavat kartā dadyāt tasmai sudakṣiṇāṃ |  
nivedyātmānikaṃdhājñāntārī vijñāpayedidi ||  
  
a *? me saphalaṃ janma yatsaṃsāra mahārṇavāt |  
  
147b)  
  
udhṛtosmiṃ tvayānātha kleśitastvaṃ kṣame svame ||  
  
tatorcitā *? ḥ kartā hṛṣṭo hṛṣṭena cārpayet |  
japārpanokta vidhinā tasmai sthāpanajasphalaṃ ||  
  
dadītāṃ pūrṇau dakṣiṇā dvaya rūpiṇīṃ |  
dīkṣā pratiṣṭā yāgānte parvanyabhyāgate tathā ||  
  
mantralābhe'tha tatsiddhau guro pūjā praśasyate |  
aṃsaṃpūjya guruṃ mohāt mūrtipānastu jāpinaḥ ||  
  
naivāpnoti phalaṃ kiñci sthāpakasyaiva tadbhavet |  
yāgomantraṃ vinācāryaṃ rāṣṭraṃ mannana varjitaḥ ||  
  
dharmañca yajamānañca hanyād dakṣiṇayā vinā |  
yāgasyopaskaraḥ pūto gurorgrāhyassamaṇḍapaḥ ||  
  
sopaskara pradhānasya śilpinaḥ snānamaṇḍapaḥ |  
svayaṃbhūte sahaśraṃ tu tadarddhandevatādibhiḥ ||  
  
pratiṣṭhite narairliṅgai kṣetraṃ haste śataṃ bhavet |  
pāpācārodhiyātyasminmṛtaḥ parami gatiṃ ||  
  
svayaṃbhūraśavāṇānāṃ kṣetraṃ sarvatra yojanaṃ |  
tathā mahānadīnāñca carācara gati pradaṃ ||  
  
149a)  
  
tadante kalpayet tīrthaṃ śivākṣaṃ śānti vāriṇā |  
revādīnāmabhāve tu tadevapāvanaṃ mahat ||  
  
devasya prāsādā bhavatu yathākāṣṭhayā kāmaṃ |  
tatpuruṣādi mukhāni tu jahati pūrvādi diksaṃsthāṃ ||  
  
liṅgaṃ vā pratimā vā kriyate nyadvāyayāpayākakṣubhāṣa tasyāṃ tasyāṃ   
yajñāyateta śivamuttarābhimukhaṃḥ ||  
  
mukhyapratiṣṭhāpanaṃ ||  
  
vidadhyāt pūrvavat sarvaṃ vāṇaliṅgai calācalau |  
nokṣilallakṣaṇaṃ cātra saṃskṛtaṃ tvāt purāmaraiḥ ||  
  
susaṃsthānaṃ visaṃsthānaṃ sarvasiddhikaraṃ sadā |  
vikalpārhaṃ na jātvena sarvaprāsādapīṭhagaṃ ||  
  
atrārthamūrtīśakalpanā kriyate na vā |  
homaśca bhūtaye nātra caturthī caṇḍakalpanā ||  
  
na mantra saṅkaro jātu sāmānyetara yogataḥ |  
calamanyadapi svatthaṃ na kvacit sthiratāṃ nayet ||  
  
rauhecitsannidhiḥ kāryaḥ saṃskāro vāṇaliṅgavat |  
  
vāṇādi ||  
  
calaliṅge pṛthak pīṭhaṃ saṃskṛtasaṃskṛte nyaśet |  
  
149b)  
  
dhyātvā jñāna kriyāśaktiṃ liṅge pīṭhekamena tu |  
sa pīṭhamapitācca kiṃ tvabhedena saskṛtaṃ ||  
  
yojayediṣṭamantraiḥstu vidhinā sphāṭikādikaṃ |  
sarvamevātra pūrvoktaṃ maṇḍape saṅgṛhethavā ||  
  
kuryād vidhau caturthyādyaṃ kiṃ bhūnunigrahe svarān |  
sāmānye tu visargaḥ syād viṣiṣṭasaṃnidhissadā ||  
  
pañcadhā vā tridhā vāpi ratnādyaṃ vibhajet purā |  
bhāgadvayamathaikaṃ vā viṃnyaśet piṇḍikā vaṭe ||  
  
addheṇa vā yathāśobhaṃ pūjābhāgo japārṇave |  
ratnajaṃ dhātu jayadvā svayonyathā viyoni vā ||  
  
liṅgapratiṣṭhaye jñātvā lakṣaṇaṃ pūrvavannavā |  
śilāratnādi vinyāśa piṇḍikāyāśca yojanaṃ ||  
  
mānasaṃ sarvamevātra śeṣaṃ pūrvoditaṃ bhavet |  
hemaraupyārasaundheṣu dāruje svāsaneṣu ca ||  
  
śuddhesūkṣīrṇa padmeṣu sviṣṭakāyāṃ samuṅgake |  
asambhave tu vastrārddha pūjyaṃ syāt takṣitau kvacit ||  
  
150a)  
  
pūjānte tat punaḥ sthāpyaṃ samudge puṣpaveṣṭita |  
śayyāśīrṣoparinaraiḥ kṛtvā sikṣesa vastrakaṃ ||  
  
skandhe kṛtvā pravāsaṣi svayamanyotha vā nayet |  
satpuṇyaphalaṃ lipsāyāṃ yāvajjivamaso vidhiḥ ||  
  
yatnena rakṣanīyaṃ tatprāyaścitta bhayāt sadā |  
sveṣṭamo darśanaṃ liṅge sāmānye cettadāmakhe ||  
  
adīkṣitānā bhūtāṃnāṃmityājñā pārameśvarī |  
  
sphāṭikādi ||  
  
vyaktārcāyāñca prāgukto vidhiścaṇḍeśvaraṃ vināḥ |  
tāsāyatsthāpanaṃ tat syāt kriyāśakti puraḥsaraṃ ||  
  
saptasaptāṅgite kharbhe caturthe brahmaṇa padaṃ |  
tṛtīyepi śurāṇāṃ syāt manuṣyāṇāṃ dvitīyake ||  
  
prathame ca piśācānāṃ vasvaṃśe bhānudurgayoḥ |  
devamanuṣye yormadhye pidhrīsthānaṃ kacottare ||  
  
tatra brahmaśilāpīṭha pṛthutvārddha pravistarāḥ |  
tadarddhenocchritā kāryā sa ratna na ca gartikāḥ ||  
  
ratnādi pañcakaṃ yanna kūrmādyaṃ pañcakīrtitaṃ |  
tatsarvaṃ kaśilā bhāve pīṭhagarte niveśayet ||  
  
150b)  
  
pitāmaha yadādhastā vicitrārthānyanu kramāt |  
rakṣomaraṇāṃrāṇā tu padāni skandha pauskare ||  
  
arccākuḍyena saṃyuktā rakṣasthāna sthitāśayā |  
śilpisthāpaka katṝṇāṃmāpūrṇasakarī bhavet ||  
  
suptāśīnorddha yāgāne khasthā cakṣmādi pañcake |  
kakārāditi hastāṃta calaukṣī pratimā kvacit ||  
  
ata ūrddhañca saṃcālyā jayādyupadravā kulā |  
vṛkṣaṇāmakṣajātīnāṃ mantrārāmasuveśmaṇāṃ ||  
  
śūle toraṇaghaṃṭānāṃ snānādyaṃ prāgvadā caret ||  
  
vyaktādi ||  
  
dhvastaśukla dṛḍhaṃ vastraṃ stambhayitvā yathā vidhiḥ |  
tasya madhyai nyaśet padme karṇikāyāṃ śadāśivaṃ ||  
  
kṛtāñjali puṭasveta mahāsarpopavītinaṃ |  
darśayet trīṇi caktrāśadyeśāno na darśayet ||  
  
īśānacchāyayā svetaṃ madhye tatpuruṣaṃ likhet |  
śitāsyaṃ projvalaṃ dhyānastimitākṣi trayaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
aghoraṃ bhīṣanaṃ daṣṭrā vikaṭānanamadbhutaṃ |  
  
151a)  
  
bhinnāñjana cayaprakhyaṃ jvannetrayotrajvalṃ |  
piṅgabhruśma śrukeśañca dakṣiṇa skandhayadyānaṃ ||  
  
vāmadevaṃ sugaurañca strīmukhābhaṃ vilāśinaṃ |  
trinetraṃ susmitaṃ sambhorvāme tilakakuṇḍalaṃ ||  
  
devādhaḥ pādamūle tu karṇikāyāṃ manonmanī |  
prāgādīśāntagā saumyāḥ śaktirvāmādikā tathā ||  
  
dakṣajānu samīpasthaṃ hṛdayaṃ vahni diggata |  
vāmajānu saṃnidhisthamīśāne ca śiro bhavet ||  
  
dakṣośanikaṭe cūḍā carmacānātmasaṃnidhau |  
pūrvādi dikṣu pītāni bhīmānyastrāni pūrvavat ||  
  
dvāreṣu varṇeṣu maṇḍaleścaturaśrake |  
śakto navāṣṭa cāṅgāni sadeśābhi mukhāni tu ||  
  
agnyādī śāntakoneṣu catuḥsiṃhānyaśe tataḥ |  
devādhastādindramevamagnādīśāntago nyaset ||  
  
īśorddhasthaṃ ca braṃhmāṇaṃ nairityūrddhepi keśavaṃ |  
rakṣovaruṇayormadhye pṛthivīṃ cāstu puruṣaṃ ||  
  
vidhiśriyau saṃsthā *? ṇānilamadhyagaṃ |  
  
151b)  
  
kṣetrapālamamīsarva dhyātavyā śivasaṃmukhāḥ |  
indradakṣiṇa *?masthau nandikālau ca prāgdiśiḥ ||  
  
stavaṃ dakṣāduttarāntaṃ bhṛgādyāścaṇḍapaścimā |  
maṇḍapasya vahissvata kartavyā vāhya hṛdayaḥ ||  
  
tadvahirgajagokarṇā dayo'nyavā vibhūṣaṇai |  
yamanairityamadhyasthaḥ kṛtāñjaliṃ puṭastu van ||  
  
devadakṣiṇato brahmāhaṃsastyāharasaṃsthitaḥ |  
tadvadyakṣānitāntastho vāmataḥstākṣaśaucyutaḥ ||  
  
śakroryekṣeśayārmadhye danāgnau bhāskarastathā |  
gaṇaṃ saraśvatīrlakṣmī kāle nandīdratopyadhaḥ ||  
  
yadvā saumya dakṣamadhye gaṇavāṇī śriyaḥ śriye |  
devadakṣe nandi gaṅge vāme kālārkaje nyaset ||  
  
yadvā gaṅgānandi yāmye yamunākālasaumyagāṃ |  
astravādho mahālakṣmyā brahāvāstvaṃtike yaḥ ||  
  
nandi vāhye svagurvādyaṃ kālavāhyena ṭādikaṃ |  
etastu paścimaṃ dvāraṃ jñeyaṃ lipi vaśāt punaḥ ||  
  
152a)  
  
sa deśādhasthitatvena pūrvameva pratīyate |  
nai-ṛtādyūrddha paṃktau ca pūrvagaṇapatiṃ likhet ||  
  
brahmāṇīṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ raudrīṃ gāyatrīṃ bhāskarīṃ kramāt |  
durgā caturitā vaidya nāthaṃ herambamicchayā ||  
  
tvaritā siṃhamāsyāmā śikhipakṣopalakṣitāḥ |  
śīrghasarvārthadādakṣa vāmābhyāṃ varadā bhayā ||  
  
svetāmṛtamayī tryakṣā padmacandrāmbujāśanā |  
ati saumyā jaṭācandra sarvābharaṇaśālinī ||  
  
caturbhujā yauvanādyā dakṣiṇe varadā bhayā |  
dhyātavyā vibhratī vā pūrṇacandrasudhāvaṭau ||  
  
mṛtyañjaya vaidyanātha mūrtireṣā mahodayā |  
kimanyadvahuvaktavyaṃ sarvāpekṣita siddhaye ||  
  
śīghradaḥ sarvasiddhināṃ hairamba sarvavighnahā |  
candrī gaurapīna saumyaḥ pañce bhāmāsi pañcadaka ||  
  
vyāghracarmā hyupavītī digvāhurbhūṣito jaṭī |  
dakṣiṇe varadaṃ mālāṃ paraśumudgaro *?ḥ ||  
  
vāmapāśā'nayaṃ muṇḍau laḍukabhājanaṃ |  
padmopaviṣṭā sahamya svetavarṇasya paśyataḥ ||  
  
pṛ *?paviṣṭā vāmena padmanyastāparāṃhrikāṃ |  
atha caṇḍāntagāṃ prāgvad gurutsvasvāhṛtī nyaśet ||  
  
yathāśobhaṃ yathāvarṇa yathāvarṇaṃ yathāsthitiḥ |  
citrāyasvā prayatnena nānāvarṇai samujvalaṃ ||  
  
ardhe hiṅgulasaṃrakṣa daṇḍikāñcalikānvitaṃ |  
upadyañcaliṃkā gūḍhaṃ daṇḍīvandhanasūtra yuk ||  
  
nirmāya manasaprītiṃ varddhana paṭamīdṛśaṃ |  
vikṣādyairdvāraṇābhiśca śuddhasnānādi cetasā ||  
  
darpaṇādiṣu vā snāpya lepu svakādivat |  
navānmilanamātrāpi ratnanyāsādi kalpayan ||  
  
na naśyati yathābhīṣṭārthaṃmarcayetā vistarenedamuktaṃ 'srīmānavī vimaleśvare   
||  
  
paṭādi ||  
  
pratisarvatrānāṃ śāṃ mantraiḥ svaśāstragaiḥ |  
svanāmādyakṣarairyadvā svarabhinnairyathocitaiḥ ||  
  
brahmāṇḍadhī prakṛtyantaṃ tritatvaṃ padmajanmanaḥ |  
  
153a)  
  
brahmaṇoṇḍe'dhikāraḥ syā bhāgo guṇātmaniḥ |  
stuprakṛtau caitaduktaṃ hiraṇya garbhake ||  
  
tanmātrā vyakta puṃtatva trayaṃ viṣṇārjayo game |  
viṣṇumūrtiḥ purasthāpyastārkṣā deva gate kṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
tatra cintatrabudhyantatrayastambhai'tha pīṭhagaḥ |  
kṣmādi garvānta nṛṣukolovalomālāṇiruddhvau ||  
  
brahmānārāyaṇo viṣṇu nṛsiṃho vāsudevavān || 9||  
  
matsyakūrmāvadāhaśca narasiṃhotha vāmanaḥ |  
ramorāmaśca rāmaśca vuddhaḥ kalki dharāditaḥ ||10||  
  
keśavo nārāyano mādhavo govindaviṣṇuve |  
madhughna trikamā *? mana śrīdhara hṛśīkeśā   
padmanābhadāmodarasya tvate kṣmādi śivāntā ||12||  
  
tryakṣaḥ umāpatisthānu nīlakaṇṭho vimohaṇe |  
mahādeva śivorudraḥ saṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ ||  
  
īśāno dhanado bhīmo rudrāḥ mārgādi kārtike ||12||  
  
kṣāmbutejo marudvyoma manobuddhirahaṃ kṛtiḥ |  
prakṛtaḥ puruṣaḥ śakti śivo'rkārudravat sthitāḥ ||12||  
  
153b)  
  
māyā sadeśaśaktyantaṃ śivadurgoṣṇarociṣāṃ |  
tritatva cānyathā tvetadyathā vīra * *? ttare ||  
  
māyeśvara sadeśvānta tritatvaṃ bhāskarasya tu |  
śaktitatve layantasya bhogo vidyā pade mahān ||  
  
adhikārāpi sūryasya śuddhādhvani sa deśavat |  
hariharārdhanārī sāmāyāntā vijayottare ||  
  
sugatasya hāraīśāna śilāyāśca nivesane |  
mātrāgarva guṇāntañca jinasya sthāpanai trayaṃ ||  
  
pṛthvī tatvasthitā nadyaḥ samudrākṣetrayā api |  
yamunā varuṇombhodhi gaṅgālakṣmīśarasvatī ||  
  
mahānadyopi pyaṃvratatvasthā svānyathā kvacit |  
nādyaśagaṇamātṝṇāṃ yakṣe bhāgya guhātmanāṃ ||  
  
aśudhīśuddhavidyānta malaṃ grāse tritatvakaṃ |  
anantādyāḥ śikhaṇḍyatā proktāḥ prokṣāpyātma tatvagāḥ ||  
  
brahmāṇi śuddhavidyāyāṃ śivāṅgāni kvacicchive |  
dharmādyā saha vidyeśaiḥ śuddhavidyā va bhāninaḥ ||  
  
sādaśāne śivāṃgāni vīrabhadrādi kīrtanāt |  
  
154a)  
  
pratiṣṭhāpyāvidhānena śivayāge cyutādayaḥ |  
śivo naivānyayāgeṣu sarvoddhorddha sthito yataḥ ||  
  
brahmādi vyāptiḥ ||  
  
dvārāṅganikasāyādi plutānyācchādyavāśasā |  
nidhāyaśayanena svatrayaṃ nyaśedyathā purā ||  
  
adhopasavyasarvordhe madhye svathakalānyaśet |  
tāśca santarpa yatnā snādvāre bindu kalāmaye ||  
  
iṣṭvānirudhya hutvā ca japtvā vāstuṃ ca dvāradhaḥ ||  
  
abhyarcyānantamanuno tatra ratnādikaṃ nyaśet |  
kṛtvāpūrvavacchānti tato rakṣārthasārvike ||  
  
gomṛdvaradarogendrayavasiddhārtha lakṣmaṇā |  
tilagorocanā krāntā vṛdvṛddha mṛtamohanā ||  
  
dadhidūrvāsahāstvāsāṃ kṛtvādau pāṭṭaliṃ guruḥ |  
vaddhorddho dumvarābjatāṃ dhruvena dhruva kalpite ||  
  
kiñciduturato nītvā dvāraṃ samyagnivesya ca |  
adho nyaśedātma tatvaṃ vidyākhyaṃ sākhayo *?yoḥ ||  
  
154b)  
  
ākāśe śivatatvaṃ tu vyāpinaṃ sarvatopiṇaṃ |  
yadvādhastādāśatānuṃ mūrtisākhāgatāṃ nya * *? ||  
  
vyāpakañca śiraṃ sāyaṃ(?) matrākhyāhuti saptakān |  
nandyādīnapi dvārasthā snātātsvavyāpti nāmabhiḥ ||  
  
setkṛtya hṛdyutaireka sutaṃ śataṃ hunedatha |  
astreṇa sūtraṃ saṃvāta doṣamoṣepi digvaliṃ ||  
  
muktaupi dahabhṛddadyāditi dvāranivaśanaṃ ||  
  
etarhidhāmadehātma sambandha kathyate sa ca |  
sakṣanā sa samāptau syā prāgvedyāṃ garbhamadhyataḥ ||  
  
svarṇaraupya maye vāpi puruṣe snānaśatkriyāḥ |  
pratiṣṭhā ca yathoddiṣṭā kāryoktāditi kaśyape ||  
  
tāmrādyeka tamaṃśāra śakṣakya śivakumbhavat |  
pañcagavyamadhukṣīra pūritaṃ gandhavāriṇā ||  
  
ghaṭaṃ hṛdayapadmābhaṃ mūrtibhūtaṃ nyaśed vṛdā |  
śitaśravastu gatvāghaṃ tatpidhānaṃ phalopamaṃ ||  
  
rakṣāṃnidhyātmatatvaṃ sarvātmābhinnarūpakaṃ |  
pūrakena tamādāya svānunākṛtakumbhakaḥ ||  
  
155a)  
  
pivājñayā bodhayitvā cintaye dvādaśāntimaṃ |  
tasmādgṛhītvā tārābhaṃ mūrtikumbhe niveśayet ||  
  
tadguṇabodhañca dehaṃ nyaṃsetatrāti vāhikaṃ |  
svākhyābhiśca nyaśettaṅkalādikṣṇāntamīśvaraiḥ ||  
  
sārddhantathā viśeṣeṇa nāḍī prāṇādikāt kramāt |  
iḍadyalambuśāntāśca mātryādaśāśavastathā ||  
  
prāṇāntāḥ kūrmākāḥ prāgvat pañcaṣaṭkarmadhīścayoḥ |  
karmendriyā viyā agni cakrācyuta caturmukhāḥ ||  
  
samitrā digmanut sṛrkhya praceto svīndavastathā |  
buddhindriyā'dhidvāttvate yojyā ijyāsvasaṃjñayā ||  
  
svakāryāpūrakatvena mādyāṃkālaniyāmikaṃ |  
svasādhyasādhakatvena vidyeśāndhrerakatvataḥ ||   
  
śivaṃ ca vyāpakatvaiva svāgaṃ svasvānuno nyaset |  
nirupyāccāthasaṃkṣepādarpyadvyāpakaṃ ghaṭaṃ ||  
  
pṛthyādita pradhānānta tatvaibhyo prakṛtaye namaḥ |  
athāsyāntarvyāpi divyaṃ namante *? mumāpatiṃ ||  
  
puṃmesaṃ nyaset sarva bhūtyaimaumiti cānunā |  
  
155b)  
  
mantrānsantarpayedeṣāṃ śānidhyecchidraśāntaye |  
  
visṛjatprathamanyastaṃ niskalaṃ vidhinā śivaṃ |  
  
hṛdaya pa *?ḥ ||  
  
īśānastanmayaḥ kāryāmūlaliṅgasamaḥ sadā |  
cūlako liṅgavadairghyādvistārādvānṛsiṃhake ||  
  
tribhakte galavistāre cūlakasārddhe dṛgguṇaḥ |  
āyāmāstryaṃ sa vistīrṇa kiñcidabhyadhikopi vā ||  
  
kaṇṭhavyāsa dalāyāma tatribhāgaika vistaraḥ |  
kvacit sārapravistārā viskambhādaśanāṃśataḥ ||  
  
yadāgrāhikayā saktyā veṣṭitaḥ kalasā kṛtiḥ |  
kumbhasyorddha triśūlañca sadasaugraha cūlakaḥ ||  
  
kumbhopari yadākaści vṛtubhāgaṃ pradarśayet |  
mūlasūnyaṃ tadetādṛksasyādīśāna kīlakaḥ ||  
  
yadākalaśasūnyasyā tribhāgaparikalpitaḥ |  
arddhadṛsyārddha śārasthastadaiva śiva cūlakaḥ ||  
  
156a)  
  
(vinā || saśyarakṣā yathākṣetraṃ sunisyanteṣu yatnataḥ |   
dharmarakṣārthamatrāpi * * *? rohastathoṣyate |   
prāsādapādavistāraṃ tadaddhardrāṃ satopi vā ||)  
  
aiṣṭakaidāruje dhāmni tvīśānādyañca dāravaṃ |  
śilāmaye mataṃ śailaṃ kvacicchuragaṇārcitaṃ ||  
  
nātra caturthikā caṇḍa kṛṣṇī prokto suparṇake |  
liṅgoktakarmayanmūrtī vaktrāṃganyāśa pūrvakaṃ ||  
  
viśeṣārtha kriyāhīnaṃ brahmabhāgārddha veśanaṃ |  
anyacca sarvaṃ pūrvoktaṃ kuryājñānīṃ kri * * *? ḥ syā   
sāddhyavā tatsamādhvajaḥ |  
jaghārcalambāṃ jaghāntā daṇḍamāno'tha vā bhavet |  
dṛḍhabhūta na *? dvastraḥ pīṭhaveśī mahādhvajaḥ ||  
  
yadvāmahīmarīmāṃrṣiddhi hasta vistarotha vā |  
yāgodaye tadarddho *? yathā prāgmathavā bhṛgau ||  
  
svadīrghaśoḍaṣāṃśena sa vistīrṇa śirāvaṇe |  
nirvāsiddhaye svatīdig * *? bhāyi kāmyataḥ ||  
  
kiñkinī cāmaropeta ūrddhaṃ svavāhanāṃkitaḥ |  
svadevarūpaṃ kiñcit svaśaktyābhūṣito ||  
  
śikharaṃ tryaṃśato jyeṣṭhe tatpādonastu madhyame |  
kanyasedūrddhamārddhena daṇḍaḥ sa * *? daḥ smṛtaḥ ||  
  
śaḍagasai hṛṣṭaiḥ sreṣṭādi kramataḥ kvacit |  
  
156b)  
  
vaṃśaje *? tsa vṛddhau syāddharmā * * * * *   
  
dṛḍhaḥ snigdho mṛduḥ sarva vṛkṣadoṣasaksitaḥ ||  
  
kalyāṇe * * *? granthirvaktra parvāpya sanmaṇi |  
āropye māne bhagnesmidrājñaska * *? yurbhavet ||  
  
tatra ghorā * * *? stiḥ kāryoktā vyāpti sadgrahaiḥ |  
dhvajadaṇḍālayaṃ pṛṣṭha tvaiśaivāmārutepi vā ||  
  
vāṇavedaguṇānsena sikhayā uttamāditaḥ |  
pūrvārdhe vāpi vā paścātsārānte dhāmni nirmite ||  
  
prāgvat snāpita gandhādye śragvastrādi sumaṇḍite |  
vinyasya dhārikāṃ śaktiṃ mūrti vaktrādi pūrvavat ||  
  
ātmavidyā śivāśeṣānjayāmadhyorddha bhāgataḥ |  
prāguktamantrairāropya jñātvā tatsannidhau hunet ||  
  
nyasyādhanyāpinaṃ saṃbhuṃ saṃnirudhya yathoditaṃ |  
anantādi pareśānta tatvaugha sadhiṣṭhitaṃ ||  
  
saṃdhadīta jagatyainaṃ liṅgapiṇḍikayā yathā |  
  
157a)  
  
saṃsnāpyāpi cūladaṇḍā vasinā prokṣayedvajaṃ |  
pūrvavatmaṇḍapādau tu śayyāstha vidhimārcayet ||  
  
śayyādi pañcakaṃ daṇḍe niskalañca śivadhvaje |  
ātmavidye punardaṇḍa śivatatvaṃ dhvaje nyaśet ||  
  
cūlake dhvajayoḥ paścāt pratibhāgañca sannidhau |  
haumayet saṃhitā mantrairddhvajārtha tu ṣaḍantakaiḥ ||  
  
susaparyanirudhyārtha brahmabhirvā śivena vā |  
śataṃ sahaśramarddhaṃ vā jñātvā japtvā nivedya ca ||  
  
ratnādikaṃ dhvajādhāre nyasya prāgvat tathāśanaṃ |  
sadyena nītvā sa mūrti bhūtaṃ daṇḍasamarpaye ||  
  
tasmin tu hyena sakalī kṛtmataṃ cātha sa dhvaje |  
śivaṃ niskalaṃ māropya sāṅgaṃ saṃpūjya yuktitaḥ ||  
  
yedhīrānyastatvānāṃ svāyudhapya *? pānayaḥ |  
tatsarvātvinyase dhyāya nantarāyā pahāriṇaḥ ||  
  
ācārya bandhu yajāpi(?) *? lambita mahādhvaje |  
lagnapradakṣiṇī kṛtya samāpnotiṃ hitaṃ phalaṃ ||  
  
ityukto kramo leṣā * * * * *? bhigaddhyate |  
prāgukte vāsane nyasya brahmāviṣṇu śivāṃśataḥ ||  
  
mūrtyādikaṃ kvacit proktaṃ śeṣa * * * *? kvacit |  
tataśca pūrva duccā(?) japtvā tatsaṃkhyayāstukaṃ ||  
  
gandhādi brahmamuṇḍena dadyādvidyā'dhipenāṃ *? |   
ṣuruṣṭhu tena naivyadyaṃ valikarma hṛdaiva tu ||  
  
prāgvacca mūrtibhūtaṃ taṃ daṇḍamastrāgavigrahaṃ |   
astrābhi mantrite dhvaja sahitaṃ saniveśayet ||  
  
pūrvoktāṅga yuktaṃ dhyāyan sahasrārka samaprabhaṃ |  
pralayāmbudanirghoṣaṃ dīpta bhruśmaśrumūrddhajaṃ ||  
  
pradīptadaśana prakāśāna na kandanaṃ |  
kruddhaṃ taḍillatā jihvaṃ sarpyāṅkadopavītakaṃ ||  
  
prāgukta dhvajavaktrādyaṃ dayitānāvimarddhakaṃ |  
prāsāda liṅgavedīnāṃ yāvanta paramānavaḥ ||  
  
tāvaskalpa śahasrāṇi kartabhoga bhujaphalaṃ |  
kṛte mahādhvajā rohe tatkoṭi guṇe taṃ bhavet ||  
  
jīrṇepi saṃskṛte puṇyamitadevasikhāmṛte ||  
  
kṣiptvāntaḥ sakalaṃ kuryālliṅgaṃ dhātujaratnajaṃ |  
  
158a)  
  
surāgāropariparaṃ bhoganirvāṇadāyakaṃ |  
māheśa caṇḍikā dhāmno śūlaṃ vā kalaśopari ||  
  
liṅgabījasamaṃ tasmāllakṣaṇāntaratopi vā |  
dvātriṃśadaṅgulaṃ śreṣṭaṃ madhyedhameṣṭabhānitaḥ ||  
  
hemaraupyamayojyaṃ vā saṃskṛtya pūrvavat tyajet |  
vāmājyeṣṭhā ca raudrī ca śaktitrayaṃ sadehakaṃ ||  
  
yadvā jñānī kriptecchākhyaṃ śaktiyuktaṃ śivārute |  
karīrapṛṣṭhabhāgena cakraṃ syādvartanaṃ dṛḍhaṃ ||  
  
jīvāyāmasamo daṇḍa tatsthaulyaṃ tajjināṃśataḥ |  
harerdvimni mataṃ hyemaṃ sūryasya vyomavāmbujaṃ ||  
  
svāyudhandhanya devānāṃ svasvamantrairnyaset sadā |  
cūlikottara devānāṃ sthāpanīyā yathā gamaṃ ||  
  
vedanāhedbhaveddhīrghā tatsthūlā cāṣṭamāśavaḥ |  
guhyasūtrādi saṃvīkṣa ityuktā sthūlakamiti ||  
  
dhvajārohaḥ ||  
  
calitaṃ cālitaṃ bhagnaṃ khaṇḍitaṃ sphuṭitaṃ ca tat |  
dagdhannyūnādhikṣonmārga tathā? saṃlakṣma * * *? ||  
  
158b)  
  
garbhapatitaṃ jīrṇaṃ savraṇapātitādipa |  
ityādi doṣavalliṅgaṃ māśrityarākṣasādayaḥ ||  
  
tasmālliṅgasamudhṛtya guṇavadyanta darpayet ||  
  
mani * * *? rai daityaistatva vidbhiḥ pratiṣṭhitaṃ |  
jīrṇavāpyatha vā bhagnaṃ vidhināpi na cālayet ||  
  
virocchannañca yalliṅga yadajñe na pratithitaṃ |  
daivajñaiḥ śilpinānyairvā śivadīkṣāṃ viva * *? ||  
  
bhūyopi tasya saṃskāraṃ kuryāt pūrvavidhānataḥ |  
aiśāne dakṣiṇe cāsyā pratyagdvāraika toraṇaḥ ||  
  
devadvāra tṛdīśena pādadhāmasumaṇḍapaḥ |  
pūrvavallokayāniṣṭvā vāstu devāṃśca duṃdubhau ||  
  
saṃpūjya sthaṇḍile śastu mantrān satarpa dīpayet |  
bhojaye liṅgināścaiva mitopendrādike dvijāḥ ||  
  
santarpyavalirirbhūtāt samadhīśca śivo yathā |  
bhagavandevadeveśa nāthadoṣāvahaṃnvidaṃ ||  
  
liṅgamasyodvṛtau śānti bhavatīti bhavedvacaḥ |  
  
159a)  
  
asyodvārāpaśāntasmādadhitiṣṭhantu saṅkaraḥ ||  
  
evakurmakiloktosau śivenāṣṭa śatādinā |  
samidurvādadhikṣīra ghṛtādyaiśāntimācaret ||  
  
ghoreṇa juhuyāliṅgaṃ cālanāya sahaśrakaṃ |  
tato liṅgāntikaṃ gatvā tatsaṃsnāpya gururyajet ||  
  
oṃ vyāpakeśvarāyeti namonto mūlavācakaḥ |  
oṃ vyāpaka hṛdayāya vyāpakaḥ śirase namaḥ ||  
  
evamantraśikhāvarma netrāstrāṇi kramena tu |  
ebhirdhruvāsane liṅgaṃ sthaṇḍilañca prapūjayet ||  
  
atha tatrāśritaṃ satvaṃ śrāvayedastramuccaran |  
satvaḥ kaupīhayakaścilliṅgamāsṛtya tiṣṭhati ||  
  
liṅgatyaktāśayatreṣṭaṃ tatrā yātu śivājñayā |  
vidyeśvarairyuktasaṃbhuratra bhaviṣyati ||  
  
ityājñāpyā tato'streṇa japtvācārghaṃ visarjayet |  
sahaśrañca * * * *? kṛtvā sastreṇa prāk kramāt ||  
  
śāntya prokṣasaṃspṛśya japtvāstra vidhinā tataḥ |  
datvā para * * * *? visṛjet mūrtiyāttikān ||  
  
159b)  
  
caṇḍesaṃ vātha hemena khaniveṇāsinākhanet |  
veṣṭā(?) svaṇḍa(?) * * * *?   
rakṣā skanda gayā dṛḍhaṃ ||  
  
vṛṣayo liṅgapīṭhaṃ vā dvayaṃ caika samastakaṃ |  
yatnādudhṛtpalokānāṃ dadet sānti vahirṇayet ||  
  
taireva sahitastoye kṣiped gṛhena vāhyadā |  
śailasnathaṭahe ghoraṃ mantra naiva tu dārujaṃ ||  
  
lohanirmāyatraiva nyaset prosvanvahaṃ sake |  
dagdhaṃ maṇi * *? bhraṣṭataṃja prastāravaṃ tyajet ||  
  
paścādvāstu sa paryoktaṃ mantrerdatvā ca digvaliṃ |  
pūrvamānānditīliṅgaṃ prāgvat saṃskṛtya garbhake ||  
  
svasthāne tu samāropya yajet mūlā vatāryavat |  
kvaciduktonyadevānāṃ vidhiścāpi niveśanaṃ ||  
  
astreṇa vā svamantreṇa sahaśraṃ juhuyāt tataḥ |  
jīrṇoddharaḥ punaḥ prāgvad vidheyaḥ siddhimicchatāḥ ||  
  
jīrṇavāma samuddhāraiḥ khaḍge vinyasya tanmanūn |  
yajet prāsāda si *? ntaṃ liṅgayatnena pālayet ||  
  
160a)  
  
siddheṣāṣyaṅgaṃ sa yogaṃ kuryādākṛṣya khaḍgataḥ |  
  
pūrvākhya khahramājīrṇastadravyaṃstat pramāṇakaḥ |  
aṣṭadravyamathaśreṣṭo'tihīnohīna vastujaḥ ||  
  
saṃkocena bhavet mṛtyu vistaraṇaṃ yayaḥ |  
jīrṇamudhṛtya cāropya prāyaścittāya homayet ||  
  
acchidra pūrṇatoyena khadadyojā?tena tu |  
kṣamayecca praṇamyaśaṃ saṃpūjya tṛṇavinduvita ||  
  
bhavāvyattā *? yotte śatvadājñayo mayo dhṛtaṃ |  
liṅgādi sthāpanaṃ yacca tatkṣamasta * *? pari ||  
  
rājñaḥ * * * * * * * * * *?   
maheśvaraḥ |  
asmākaśilpino nyeṣāṃ suprītā bhavata bhavaḥ ||  
  
tataḥ karṇa * * * * * * * * * * *   
taṅkhaḍgaṃ? kaṃkanaṃ dhenuṃ dadyāt sopiṣkarau vṛṣau ||  
  
ī * *? rṇe dvāraṃ ||  
  
maṭhata * *? nāṃ kuryā *? sā dadviguṇā mahīṃ |  
jagatī vāhyato hitvā dakṣa * *? 'thavāruṇe ||  
  
pūrvavatsaṃ * *? kuryātkuṇḍamaṇḍa *? maṇḍapaṃ |  
  
160b)  
  
iṣṭvā śivaghaṭaṃ liptvā sa * * * * * * *? |  
  
vipraḥ purassarai naiva samaṃ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ |  
pra * * * * * * *? dvilavyā tu praviśya ca ||  
  
catuske dhānyadhuṃjorddhe kumbhaṃ nyasyodagānanaṃ |  
dvija * * * * * * * * * * * *   
  
jagatī ma * * * * * * * * * *?   
kalāḥ ||  
  
prāgukta vyāptya * * * *? sva * * hṛdādayet ||  
  
tato sadamatvā vāstu devatāt tarpyatān |  
kalāśca dvādhyakṣāṃśca pratiṣṭhārthaṃ tu tarpayet ||  
  
dattadidi * lirācāntantu kāyo vibhūṣite |  
maṭhaṃ sasnāpayedasra bījapūraka pitthakaiḥ ||  
  
vadarī phalavārtākta mātataṃ nāraṅgakaiḥ |  
dāḍimā malakaiḥ kandaiḥ kumbhābhobhi'sca bhūribhiḥ ||  
  
maṭhedya śrīvayatnāmakartuḥ *? di vṛddhaye |  
  
161a)  
  
pāśaskandaṃ paśuskanda vidyāsākheśvaracchadaṃ |  
śaktipuṣpasukhānatya phalavande śivahramaṃ ||  
  
ṣaṭpuṣpe teṣu vidhiṣu yatkiṃcit nādita mayā |  
tajjñeya vimalāvatyā sarvasvāśaiva me yataḥ ||  
  
naitacchivoktaṃ *? tyatranādheyaḥ saṃ * *? kvacit |  
ānakyānastato(?) vartu tathā keṃdrodayopyalaṃ ||  
  
śrīmadguru praca *? pādasahaśrarasmi * *?   
trividhavandhamaṇḍāndhakāraḥ(?) |  
kāṇyāṃ ca sa vimalaśambhurasambhava śrīvi *? rāṃ hri yugapaṅkaja   
vañca * * *? yaḥ sa * * * *   
ślokamuktakolkīrṇavigrahaṃ |   
  
mantrakaṇṭhakasaṃśuddhāṃ guruparāgatāḥ |  
cakre nātmapakṣa * * * * *? paddhatiṃ sakhayaitāṃ ||  
  
pāpagrāme saranye paśupate supateḥ śiṣṭābudhya praveśaḥ |  
yatkiñcit * *? masyāṃ sakalajanahinirmitāyāmabhūtme ||  
  
tena prīta śivombhū prabhurati karuṇā nirguṇa ṣaṭguṇa śrīḥ |  
haktomayeṣadvipamārthaṃ(?) saṃśrī * * * * *   
  
161b)   
  
ūnclear
